```java
    GamePanel(RuntimeProfile runtimeProfile, boolean startTimer) {

        this.launcherShell = new LauncherShellStateAuthority(this.runtimeProfile);
```

```java
    void updateDynamicMusic(String reason) {
        if (sounds == null) return;
        String key = desiredMusicContext();
        sounds.requestMusic(key, options);
        if (!key.equals(lastMusicAuditKey) || (reason != null && reason.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("combat"))) {
            lastMusicAuditKey = key;
            DebugLog.audit("MUSIC_ROUTE", "reason=" + reason + " key=" + key + " screen=" + screen + (world == null ? "" : " zone=" + world.zoneType.label) + " combatUntil=" + combatMusicUntilTurn + " governorUntil=" + governorBattleMusicUntilTurn + " turn=" + turn);
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:145-157
Kind: method
Name: desiredMusicContext
SHA256: 37cc4a095ccdf4eeaa6f906b4589ac7fe77cab33518349ad51ac89052ecbf9cd

```java
    String desiredMusicContext() {
        if (options == null || !options.musicEnabled || options.musicVolume <= 0) return DynamicMusicManager.SILENCE;
        if (screen == Screen.BOOT) return DynamicMusicManager.SILENCE;
        if (screen == Screen.MENU || screen == Screen.OPTIONS || screen == Screen.LOST) return "MAIN_MENU";
        if (screen == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) return DynamicMusicManager.SILENCE;
        if (screen == Screen.CHARACTER || screen == Screen.KNOWLEDGE || screen == Screen.WORLD_SELECT || screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP || (screen == Screen.LOADING && loadingForNewGame)) return "CHARACTER_SELECT";
        if (screen == Screen.GAME || screen == Screen.PANEL || screen == Screen.PAUSE || screen == Screen.ZONE_SPLASH || screen == Screen.LOADING) {
            if (governorBattleMusicUntilTurn > turn || hostileGovernorPressureNearby()) return "ESTATE_BATTLE";
            if (combatMusicUntilTurn > turn || hostilePressureNearby()) return "COMBAT";
            return zoneAmbientMusicContext();
        }
        return "LOW_HABITATION";
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:273-294
Kind: method
Name: setScreen
SHA256: f23d07bb78f23a9011ccb362a24891c2cfefa6f297777d404ee9c9758732719c

```java
    void setScreen(Screen next) {
        Screen oldScreen = screen;
        PanelMode oldPanel = panelMode;
        if (screen != next) previousScreen = screen;
        if (next == Screen.PANEL || next == Screen.OPTIONS || next == Screen.PAUSE) sounds.play("panelOpen", options);
        if (oldScreen == Screen.PANEL && next != Screen.PANEL) clearExpiredPanelState(oldPanel, "screen change to " + next);
        if (oldScreen == Screen.OPTIONS && next != Screen.OPTIONS) clearExpiredOptionsState("screen change to " + next);
        if (oldScreen == Screen.PAUSE && next != Screen.PAUSE) clearExpiredPauseState("screen change to " + next);
        if (oldScreen == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL && next != Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) sounds.stopIntroCrawlNarration("screen change to " + next);
        if (next == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) {
            introCrawlStartMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
            if (introCrawlLines.isEmpty()) introCrawlLines = images.loadIntroCrawlLines();
            sounds.playIntroCrawlNarration(options);
            DebugLog.audit("INTRO_CRAWL_BEGIN", "lines=" + introCrawlLines.size() + " queuedZoneSplash=" + introCrawlQueuedZoneSplash + " textTargetMs=" + INTRO_CRAWL_TEXT_TARGET_MS + " audioExpectedMs=" + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_EXPECTED_MS + " audioTailSafetyMs=" + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_TAIL_SAFETY_MS);
        }
        screen = next;
        selectedButton = 0;
        activeScrollTag = "";
        requestFocusInWindow();
        updateDynamicMusic("screen change to " + next);
        repaint();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:296-336
Kind: method
Name: clearExpiredPanelState
SHA256: fe2a5fcf851a418f285fea6ccd5a135eaa9f07d1e20377de13c906a7e90bd679

```java
    void clearExpiredPanelState(PanelMode expired, String reason) {
        if (expired == PanelMode.NONE) return;
        DebugLog.audit("UI_CLOSE", "Clearing expired panel " + expired + " due to " + reason + " | " + stateSummary());
        activeScrollTag = "";
        scrollbarDragActive = false;
        if (expired == PanelMode.LOOK) {
            lookCursorActive = false;
            lookStackIndex = 0;
            lookX = playerX;
            lookY = playerY;
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.COMBAT) {
            combatCursorActive = false;
            combatX = combatY = -1;
            lastTargetingReport = "No target selected.";
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.INTERACT) {
            interactCursorActive = false;
            pendingInteractionSummary = "No interaction selected.";
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.BUILD || expired == PanelMode.WORKBENCH) {
            buildPlacementActive = false;
            pendingBuildRecipe = null;
            pendingBuildSummary = "No build selected.";
            buildX = -1;
            buildY = -1;
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.TRADE) {
            activeTrader = null;
            selectedTradeOffer = 0;
            conversationBranch = "No active conversation.";
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.INTERACT || expired == PanelMode.TRADE) {
            activeConversationNpc = null;
        }
        if (expired == PanelMode.INFOPEDIA) {
            infopediaScroll = 0;
            infopediaDetailScroll = 0;
        }
        if (panelMode == expired) panelMode = PanelMode.NONE;
    }
```

```java
    void openPanel(PanelMode mode) {
        panelMode = mode;
        setScreen(Screen.PANEL);
        if (mode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH && universalWindowAuthority != null) {
            universalWindowAuthority.open("machine_operations", turn, "workbench machine-operation status bridge");
            DebugLog.audit("MACHINE_OPERATION_STATUS_BRIDGE", MachineOperationStatusBridge.compactSummary(this));
            DebugLog.audit("STAFFING_LABOR_BRIDGE", StaffingLaborBridgeAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            }
        logEvent("Opened panel: " + mode);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:362-372
Kind: method
Name: closePanel
SHA256: f899d0832961f8d7366f375ad18a7c92c4134875cb1f84aee28baae52d1da7e1

```java
    void closePanel() {
        sounds.play("panelClose", options);
        PanelMode closing = panelMode;
        clearExpiredPanelState(panelMode, "explicit close");
        if (!lookCursorActive) { lookX = playerX; lookY = playerY; }
        if (previousScreen == Screen.LOST) setScreen(Screen.LOST);
        else if (previousScreen == Screen.MENU || previousScreen == Screen.PAUSE || previousScreen == Screen.OPTIONS || previousScreen == Screen.WORLD_SELECT || previousScreen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP || previousScreen == Screen.CHARACTER) setScreen(previousScreen);
        else if (previousScreen == Screen.MODS || previousScreen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) setScreen(previousScreen);
        else if (world == null && closing == PanelMode.SAVELOAD) setScreen(Screen.MENU);
        else setScreen(Screen.GAME);
    }
```

```java
    boolean recentActionEligible(String s) {
        if (s == null || s.isBlank()) return false;
        String low = s.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (low.startsWith("opened panel:") || low.startsWith("closed panel:") || low.startsWith("benchmark") || low.startsWith("metric/") || low.startsWith("audit/") || low.startsWith("settings/") || low.startsWith("debug") || low.contains("worstpaintms") || low.contains("renderprofile=") || low.contains("current.log") || low.contains("runtime.log") || low.contains("errors.log")) return false;
        if (low.contains("viewport zoom") || low.contains("world zoom") || low.startsWith("graphics dropdown") || low.startsWith("font scale") || low.startsWith("gui scale") || low.startsWith("tile icon rendering") || low.startsWith("screensaver") || low.startsWith("floating hover help") || low.startsWith("move preview") || low.contains("movement ghost") || low.startsWith("selected inventory") || low.startsWith("inventory item selected") || low.startsWith("equipment: selected")) return false;
        if (low.contains("route selected:") || low.contains("launcher shell") || low.contains("authority=") || low.contains("local-server boundary") || low.contains("zone audit generated") || low.contains("not-yet-implemented")) return false;
        return true;
    }
```

```java
    String stateSummary() {
        String activeText = active == null ? "none" : active.name + "/" + active.job;
        String worldText = world == null ? "none" : (world.w + "x" + world.h + " seed=" + world.seed);
        return "screen=" + screen + " panel=" + panelMode + " selectedButton=" + selectedButton
                + " active=" + activeText + " world=" + worldText + " player=" + playerX + "," + playerY
                + " look=" + lookX + "," + lookY + " lookActive=" + lookCursorActive
                + " turn=" + turn + " worldTurn=" + worldTurn + " heat=" + gangHeat + " suspicion=" + suspicion + " xp=" + xp + " knowledgeCredits=" + knowledgeCredits
                + " food=" + food + " water=" + water + " script=" + carriedScript + " banked=" + totalBankedCash() + " baseScript=" + baseStashedScript
                + " sleepNeed=" + sleepNeed + "/" + MAX_SLEEP_NEED + " stimStrain=" + stimulantStrain
                + " bleeding=" + bleeding + " infectionRisk=" + infectionRisk + " pain=" + pain
                + " inventory=" + inventory.size() + " storage=" + baseStorage.size() + " recruits=" + factionRecruits.size() + "/" + recruitCapacity()
                + " factionPressure=" + highestFactionMarketPressureLine()
                + " base=" + (baseClaimed ? baseX + "," + baseY + " room=" + claimedRoomId : "none")
                + " baseObjects=" + baseObjects.size() + " build=" + (pendingBuildRecipe == null ? "none" : pendingBuildRecipe.name + "@" + buildX + "," + buildY) + " visible=" + lastVisibleCount + " heard=" + lastHeardCount
                + " sectorRuntime=" + (singlePlayerSectorBridge == null ? "none" : singlePlayerSectorBridge.statusLine());
    }
```

SHA256: e433aac12da0df08d5a419e816e560c7836d3e8cdb15a740aa7892fd7179c9a6

```java
    void maybeAutosave(String reason) {
        if (active == null || world == null || atlas == null || screen == Screen.LOST) return;
        if (turn <= 0 || turn == lastAutosaveTurn) return;
        if (turn % AUTOSAVE_INTERVAL_TURNS != 0) return;
        try {
            writeSaveFile(AUTOSAVE_HOURLY_SLOT, true);
            lastAutosaveTurn = turn;
            logEvent("AUTOSAVE: hourly save at turn " + turn + " after " + reason + ".");
        } catch (Throwable t) {
            DebugLog.error("AUTOSAVE_FAILED", "Hourly autosave failed at turn " + turn + " reason=" + reason, t);
            logEvent("AUTOSAVE WARNING: could not write hourly autosave. Diagnostic details were recorded.");
        }
    }
```

```java
        if (active == null || world == null || atlas == null || screen == Screen.LOST) return;

            writeSaveFile(AUTOSAVE_ZONE_SLOT, true);

        } catch (Throwable t) {
            DebugLog.error("AUTOSAVE_ZONE_FAILED", "Zone-transition autosave failed at turn " + turn + " reason=" + reason, t);
            logEvent("AUTOSAVE WARNING: could not write zone-transition autosave. Diagnostic details were recorded.");
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:524-543
Kind: method
Name: loadGameSlot
SHA256: bfd22729b21a49bcd5fdae41557a0c5c44cb122d66593aa4d27b14ec286eec75

```java
    void loadGameSlot(int slot) {
        runGuarded("LOAD", "slot=" + slot, () -> {
            Path file = savePathForSlot(slot);
            if (!Files.exists(file)) { logEvent("No save file found for " + slotLabel(slot) + " at " + file.toString() + "."); return; }
            Properties pr = new Properties();
            try { try (InputStream in = Files.newInputStream(file)) { pr.load(in); } } catch (IOException ex) { throw new RuntimeException(ex); }
            SaveEfficiencyAuthority.mergeReferencedWorldState(pr);
            loadingForNewGame = false;
            loadingForTransition = false;
            loadingProgress = 0;
            loadingStep = 0;
            loadingStartMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
            loadingStatus = "Loading saved underhive state.";
            Persistence.readCore(this, pr);
            updateSensoryModel("load " + slotLabel(slot));
            logEvent("Loaded " + slotLabel(slot) + ": " + stateSummary());
            DebugLog.audit("LOAD_COMPLETE", "slot=" + slot + " file=" + file.toAbsolutePath() + " keys=" + pr.size() + " state=" + stateSummary());
            setScreen(Screen.GAME);
        });
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard2.txt:554-569
Kind: method
Name: sanityCheck
SHA256: be59507f11ce81b19e23cb876e335094889eef26abe5f7f73ca523471064a481

```java
    void sanityCheck(String system) {
        if (selectedButton < 0) {
            DebugLog.warn(system, "selectedButton below zero; correcting. " + stateSummary());
            selectedButton = 0;
        }
        if (buttons.size() > 0 && selectedButton >= buttons.size()) {
            DebugLog.warn(system, "selectedButton outside button list; correcting. buttons=" + buttons.size() + " " + stateSummary());
            selectedButton = buttons.size() - 1;
        }
        if ((screen == Screen.GAME || screen == Screen.PANEL) && world == null) {
            DebugLog.warn(system, "Game/panel screen active without world. " + stateSummary());
        }
        if (world != null && (playerX < 0 || playerY < 0 || playerX >= world.w || playerY >= world.h)) {
            DebugLog.warn(system, "Player outside world bounds. " + stateSummary());
        }
    }
```

```java
        buttons.clear();
        int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
        if (eulaGateActive) {
            // 0.9.10ip: keep hitboxes locked to the same panel geometry used by drawEulaOverlay().
            // The earlier 760px rebuild frame could drift away from the wider rendered legal panel.
            int panelW = Math.min(980, Math.max(560, w - 80));
            int panelH = Math.min(720, Math.max(420, h - 80));
            int x = (w - panelW) / 2;
            int y = (h - panelH) / 2;
            int bh = 40;
            int buttonY = y + panelH - 62;

            int exitW = 130;
            int totalW = agreeW + declineW + exitW + gap * 2;
            int startX = x + panelW - totalW - 46;
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("I AGREE", startX, buttonY, agreeW, bh, "Accept the local EULA notice and write persistent consent.", this::acceptEulaGate));
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("I DO NOT AGREE", startX + agreeW + gap, buttonY, declineW, bh, "Decline the notice and close the program immediately.", () -> requestApplicationExit("EULA declined")));
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("EXIT", startX + agreeW + gap + declineW + gap, buttonY, exitW, bh, "Decline the notice and close the program immediately.", () -> requestApplicationExit("EULA exited")));
            return;
        }
        if (screen == Screen.BOOT) {
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("SKIP BOOT", w-190, h-72, 160, 38, "Bypass the logic Engine-style boot sequence and go to the main menu.", () -> finishBootSequence("button")));
        } else if (screen == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) {
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox("SKIP", Math.max(24, w-142), Math.max(24, h-66), 112, 32, "Skip the cinematic crawl and enter the generated zone.", () -> continueFromIntroCrawl()));
        } else if (screen == Screen.MENU) {
            Rectangle menuFrame = mainMenuButtonFrameRect();
            int innerPad = Math.max(12, Math.min(20, w / 86));
            int gap = Math.max(8, Math.min(14, w / 92));
            java.util.List<LauncherShellStateAuthority.RouteDescriptor> routes = launcherShell.menuRoutes(userProfile);
            ArrayList<LauncherShellStateAuthority.RouteDescriptor> gridRoutes = new ArrayList<>();
            LauncherShellStateAuthority.RouteDescriptor exitRoute = null;
            for (LauncherShellStateAuthority.RouteDescriptor route : routes) {
                if (route.route == LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.PROFILE) continue;
                if (route.route == LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.EXIT) { exitRoute = route; continue; }
                gridRoutes.add(route);
            }
            int cols = gridRoutes.size() >= 7 ? 4 : (gridRoutes.size() >= 5 ? 3 : 2);
            int rows = Math.max(1, (int)Math.ceil(gridRoutes.size() / (double)Math.max(1, cols)));
            // 0.9.10ip: reserve a complete footer band for EXIT instead of center-stacking it
            // into the grid. This prevents the multiplayer row from being overwritten at 16:9.
            int exitH = Math.max(26, Math.min(34, menuFrame.height / 5));
            int footerGap = Math.max(10, gap + 2);
            int gridTop = menuFrame.y + innerPad;
            int exitY = menuFrame.y + menuFrame.height - innerPad - exitH;
            int gridH = Math.max(24, exitY - footerGap - gridTop);
            int cellW = Math.max(82, (menuFrame.width - innerPad * 2 - gap * Math.max(0, cols - 1)) / Math.max(1, cols));
            int cellH = Math.max(23, Math.min(34, (gridH - gap * Math.max(0, rows - 1)) / Math.max(1, rows)));
            int usedGridH = rows * cellH + Math.max(0, rows - 1) * gap;
            int gridY = gridTop + Math.max(0, (gridH - usedGridH) / 2);
            for (int i=0; i<gridRoutes.size(); i++) {
                LauncherShellStateAuthority.RouteDescriptor route = gridRoutes.get(i);
                int col = i % cols;
                int row = i / cols;
                int bx = menuFrame.x + innerPad + col * (cellW + gap);
                int by = gridY + row * (cellH + gap);
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox(route.label, bx, by, cellW, cellH, route.tip, launcherMenuAction(route.route)));
            }
            if (exitRoute != null) {
                int exitW = Math.max(120, Math.min(220, menuFrame.width / 3));
                int exitX = menuFrame.x + (menuFrame.width - exitW) / 2;
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox(exitRoute.label, exitX, exitY, exitW, exitH, exitRoute.tip, launcherMenuAction(exitRoute.route)));
```

Source: gamepanel-shard3.txt:173-195
Kind: method
Name: activateCommand
SHA256: 088f7ccb46d254a51c0e01dc52747103cba3b0af477def22b19aacd6091b1c25

```java
    void activateCommand(String label) {
        sounds.play("button", options);
        switch(label) {
            case "WAIT": waitOneTurn(); break;
            case "MOVE MODE": cycleMovementMode(); break;
            case "PLAN MOVE": beginManualMovementPlan(); break;
            case "LOOK": interactCursorActive=false; lookX=playerX; lookY=playerY; lookCursorActive=true; openPanel(PanelMode.LOOK); break;
            case "INTERACT": beginInteractMode(); break;
            case "COMBAT": beginCombatTargeting(); break;
            case "INVENTORY": openPanel(PanelMode.INVENTORY); break;
            case "CHARACTER": openPanel(PanelMode.CHARACTER); break;
            case "BUILD": openPanel(PanelMode.BUILD); break;
            case "BASES": openPanel(PanelMode.BASES); break;
            case "WORK": if (hasBaseObject('w')) openPanel(PanelMode.WORKBENCH); else logEvent("No Scrap Workbench built yet. Build one before using WORK."); break;
            case "SENSES": openPanel(PanelMode.SENSES); break;
            case "MAP": openPanel(PanelMode.MAP); break;
            case "NEWS": openPanel(PanelMode.NEWS); break;
            case "LOG": openPanel(PanelMode.LOG); break;
            case "CHAT": openChatWindow(); break;
            case "SAVE/LOAD": openPanel(PanelMode.SAVELOAD); break;
            case "MENU": setScreen(Screen.PAUSE); break;
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard3.txt:199-208
Kind: method
Name: beginInteractMode
SHA256: d2887a20a72570f64e5f897781a0e99442c196e86a69838632495ccc3dadab13

```java
    void beginInteractMode() {
        if (world == null) return;
        interactCursorActive = true;
        // Default to the tile underfoot if it has an object, otherwise the eastern adjacent tile.
        if (baseObjectAt(playerX, playerY) != null || world.tiles[playerX][playerY] != '.') { lookX = playerX; lookY = playerY; }
        else { lookX = Math.min(world.w - 1, playerX + 1); lookY = playerY; }
        clampInteractCursorToAdjacent();
        updatePendingInteractionSummary();
        openPanel(PanelMode.INTERACT);
    }
```

```java
    String petAdoptionSaleReadLine(NpcEntity npc, int tx, int ty) {
        if (npc == null || !npc.isPetActor()) return "not a companion adoption target.";
        String context = (describeTile(world != null && world.inBounds(tx, ty) ? world.tiles[tx][ty] : ' ') + " " + roomContextReadLine(tx, ty) + " " + ownershipText(tx, ty)).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (context.contains("market") || context.contains("shop") || context.contains("stall")) return "possible vendor or adoption context, but no purchase is confirmed until a trade/service option says so.";
        if (npc.companionOf != null && !npc.companionOf.isBlank()) return "already bonded to a handler; not for sale from this screen.";
        return "no adoption or sale offer is visible from here.";
    }
```

SHA256: bd9e8c8fbdf34150cc781b60f001a6db3d3057bd134dd025e48e224fabab6946

```java
    void handlePlayerUnconsciousness(String cause, String attacker, String weapon, boolean theftRisk) {
        if (screen == Screen.LOST) return;
        runUnconsciousEvents++;
        int stolenItems = 0;
        int stolenScript = 0;
        if (theftRisk) {
            stolenScript = unconsciousScriptLoss();
            if (stolenScript > 0) carriedScript = Math.max(0, carriedScript - stolenScript);
            stolenItems = unconsciousItemLoss();
        }
        Point wake = unconsciousWakePoint();
        playerX = wake.x; playerY = wake.y; lookX = playerX; lookY = playerY;
        fatigue = Math.max(0, Math.min(10, fatigue / 2));
        sleepNeed = 0;
        pain = Math.max(0, pain / 2);
        bleeding = 0;
        wounds = Math.max(0, wounds - 2);
        if (active != null && active.body != null) healWorstBodyPart(25.0);
        updateSensoryModel("unconscious relocation");
        DebugLog.audit("PLAYER_UNCONSCIOUS", "cause=" + cause + " attacker=" + attacker + " weapon=" + weapon + " scriptLost=" + stolenScript + " inventoryLost=" + stolenItems + " wake=" + playerX + "," + playerY + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent("UNCONSCIOUS: " + cause + ". You are carried, dragged, ransomed, or simply found later and wake at " + wakePointLabel(wake) + ".");
        if (stolenScript > 0) logEvent("SCRIPT STOLEN: " + stolenScript + " Concord Script was lifted from your pockets while you were out.");
        if (stolenItems > 0) logEvent("ITEMS LOST: " + stolenItems + " carried item(s) were gone when you woke.");
        maybeAutosave("unconscious recovery");
    }
```

SHA256: 881c715ca28c2002f744e477fccc5c10132367d27893a1c2f703fbd69079da5e

```java
    void evaluatePlayerDefeatState(String cause, String attacker, String weapon, String location) {
        if (screen == Screen.LOST || active == null) return;
        if (shouldPlayerDieNow()) {
            triggerPlayerDeath(cause, attacker, weapon, location);
        } else if (shouldPlayerFallUnconsciousNow()) {
            if (arbitesAuthorityText(attacker) || arbitesAuthorityText(weapon)) handleArbitesCapture("incapacitated by Civic Wardens authority", Math.max(2, suspicion / 4 + wounds / 6));
            else handlePlayerUnconsciousness(cause, attacker, weapon, false);
        }
    }
```

```java
    void triggerPlayerDeath(String cause, String attacker, String weapon, String location) {
        if (screen == Screen.LOST) return;
        PlayerLifecycleService.DeathResolution deathResolution = playerLifecycleService.resolveDeath(this, cause, attacker, weapon, location);
        DebugLog.audit("PLAYER_LIFECYCLE", playerLifecycleService.statusLine(this) + " deathOutcome=" + deathResolution.outcome());
        lastDefeatCause = cause == null || cause.isBlank() ? "unknown fatality" : cause;
        lastDefeatAttacker = attacker == null || attacker.isBlank() ? "unknown" : attacker;
        lastDefeatWeapon = weapon == null || weapon.isBlank() ? "unknown" : weapon;
        lastDefeatLocation = location == null || location.isBlank() ? "unknown" : location;
        lastDefeatSummary = active.name + " was killed by " + lastDefeatAttacker + " using " + lastDefeatWeapon + " (" + lastDefeatCause + ").";
        lastLossScoreLines = PlayerDefeatAndScoreAuthority.lossScoreLines(this);
        DebugLog.audit("PLAYER_DEATH", "cause=" + lastDefeatCause + " attacker=" + lastDefeatAttacker + " weapon=" + lastDefeatWeapon + " location=" + lastDefeatLocation + " score=" + PlayerDefeatAndScoreAuthority.score(this) + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent("DEATH: " + lastDefeatSummary + " Survival time " + timeText() + ", turn " + turn + ".");
        setScreen(Screen.LOST);
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void advanceTurnBody(String reason) {
        long profileStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
        try {
        advancePlayerAndWorldTime(1, reason);
        if (turn % (4 * TURNS_PER_HOUR) == 0) gangHeat++;
        if (turn % (6 * TURNS_PER_HOUR) == 0) fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + 1);
        if (baseClaimed && turn % (5 * TURNS_PER_HOUR) == 0) suspicion++;
        passiveBaseObjectTicks();
        processProgressiveConstructionSites(false);
        applyHourlyProgressionTick(false);
        applyBusinessPressureTick(false);
        applyFactionMarketPressureTick(false);
        applyFactionStrategicSimulationTick(false);
        processExplosiveAndCorpseEcologyTick();
        processPortableLightTick();
        applyAwakeSurvivalTick();
        applyStarvationDamageIfNeeded();
        applyMedicalProgressionTick();
        decayTemporaryHostilities();
        tickNearbyNpcs();
        applyBankManagerSchedules();
        applyBankAlarmPressureTick();
        applyArbitesPatrolSweep();
        applyAuthorityFacilityInspectionFromNews();
        enforceEntityOccupancy("advance-turn");
        processPersonnelReplacementQueue();
        processMachineOperationQueueTick(false);
        updateSensoryModel("turn " + turn);
        evaluateFactionPressure();
        evaluatePlayerDefeatState("survival attrition", "the underhive", "hunger, thirst, bleeding, infection, or exhaustion", "whole body");
        if (screen != Screen.LOST) maybeAutosave(reason);
        if (active != null) logEvent(active.name + " " + reason + " Time " + timeText() + " (turn " + turn + "). Heat " + gangHeat + ", suspicion " + suspicion + ".");
        } finally {
            profilingAdvanceTurnNanos += Math.max(0L, System.nanoTime() - profileStartNanos);
            profilingAdvanceTurnSamples++;
            deferredSimulationDebt = Math.min(100000, deferredSimulationDebt + 1);
            if (turn > 0 && turn % 250 == 0) auditSimulationEfficiency("turn-sample");
        }
    }
```

```java
    void maybePlayCoreAmbientCue(long now) {
        if (screen != Screen.GAME || world == null || options == null || !options.soundEnabled) return;
        int idleBonus = (now - lastInputMillis > 1800L) ? CORE_AMBIENT_IDLE_BONUS_MS : 0;
        if (now - lastAmbientCueMillis < Math.max(900, CORE_AMBIENT_MIN_INTERVAL_MS - idleBonus)) return;
        double chance = (now - lastInputMillis > 1800L) ? 0.24 : 0.13;
        if (rng.nextDouble() > chance) return;
        lastAmbientCueMillis = now;
        String key = coreAmbientCueForZone();
        int pseudoDistance = 4 + rng.nextInt(18);
        sounds.playDistantCue(key, pseudoDistance, options);
        DebugLog.audit("CORE_AMBIENT_CUE", "key=" + key + " distance=" + pseudoDistance + " zone=" + world.zoneType.label + " idleMs=" + (now-lastInputMillis) + " turn=" + turn);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard4.txt:1061-1080
Kind: method
Name: attemptPlayerMove
SHA256: 348d4226771d99a08749898340645bba336602731212c7a1d194f1950e5dfc91

```java
    boolean attemptPlayerMove(int dx, int dy) {
        if (world == null) return false;
        updateMoveGhostTarget(dx, dy);
        int steps = movementModeRange();
        boolean movedAny = false;
        for (int i=0; i<steps; i++) {
            int nx = playerX + dx, ny = playerY + dy;
            boolean directClear = stepIsClearForPath(nx, ny);
            boolean moved = directClear ? attemptPlayerMoveOneTile(dx, dy) : attemptPlayerPathSeekingStep(dx, dy);
            if (!moved) break;
            movedAny = true;
            if (screen == Screen.LOST || world == null) break;
            // Multi-tile movement remains conservative around entity contact.  If the next
            // target is occupied, stop here so shove/push-past is deliberate, not automated.
            nx = playerX + dx; ny = playerY + dy;
            if (world.inBounds(nx, ny) && world.npcAt(nx, ny) != null) break;
        }
        updateMoveGhostTarget(dx, dy);
        return movedAny;
    }
```

```java
    void beginCombatTargeting() {
        if (world == null || active == null) { logEvent("Combat failed: no active world or character is loaded."); return; }
        explosiveTargetingMode = false;
        selectedExplosiveItem = "";
        combatCursorActive = true;
        combatX = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.w-1, playerX + Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, lastMoveDx))));
        combatY = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.h-1, playerY + Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, lastMoveDy))));
        if (combatX == playerX && combatY == playerY) combatX = Math.min(world.w-1, playerX + 1);
        lookCursorActive = false;
        interactCursorActive = false;
        lastTargetingReport = "Targeting reticle armed. Move reticle; Enter/Space confirms; F cycles fire mode; G throws a carried explosive.";
        openPanel(PanelMode.COMBAT);
    }
```

```java
    void beginExplosiveTargeting() {
        if (world == null || active == null) { logEvent("EXPLOSIVE TARGETING failed: no active world or character."); return; }
        String item = firstCarriedExplosiveItem();
        if (item.isBlank()) { logEvent("EXPLOSIVE TARGETING: no carried grenade, mine, satchel, claymore, plasma bomb, or melta grenade."); return; }
        combatCursorActive = true;
        explosiveTargetingMode = true;
        selectedExplosiveItem = item;
        combatX = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.w-1, playerX + Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, lastMoveDx)) * Math.max(2, Math.min(6, explosiveThrowRange(item)))));
        combatY = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.h-1, playerY + Math.max(-1, Math.min(1, lastMoveDy)) * Math.max(2, Math.min(6, explosiveThrowRange(item)))));
        if (combatX == playerX && combatY == playerY) combatX = Math.min(world.w-1, playerX + 3);
        lookCursorActive = false;
        interactCursorActive = false;
        lastTargetingReport = "Explosive reticle armed for " + item + ". Move reticle; G/Enter throws or plants depending on explosive type.";
```

```java
    void clearVisibleTiles(Rectangle rect) {
        if (world == null || visibleTiles == null) return;
        if (rect == null || rect.width >= world.w || rect.height >= world.h) {
            for (int x=0; x<world.w; x++) for (int y=0; y<world.h; y++) visibleTiles[x][y] = false;
            profilingVisibilityFullClears++;
            return;
        }
        int x0 = Math.max(0, rect.x), y0 = Math.max(0, rect.y);
        int x1 = Math.min(world.w-1, rect.x + rect.width - 1), y1 = Math.min(world.h-1, rect.y + rect.height - 1);
        for (int x=x0; x<=x1; x++) for (int y=y0; y<=y1; y++) visibleTiles[x][y] = false;
        profilingVisibilityLocalClears++;
    }
```

Name: applyArbitesPatrolSweep
SHA256: 6a780c768415de1ad450f08a4606addf5f5debd8d746bfd0d5490f49f50615fa

```java
    void applyArbitesPatrolSweep() {
        if (screen == Screen.LOST || screen == Screen.CAPTURE || active == null || world == null) return;
        if (!arbitesNobleOrCivilZone()) return;
        if (turn < arbitesInspectionCooldownUntilTurn) return;
        int pressure = Math.max(0, suspicion) + Math.max(0, gangHeat / 2);
        if (world.zoneType == ZoneType.ARBITES_PRECINCT_EDGE) pressure += 5;
        if (world.zoneType == ZoneType.SECTOR_GOVERNORS_MANSION || world.zoneType == ZoneType.NOBLE_SERVICE_SPINE) pressure += 3;
        if (pressure < 6) return;
        if (turn % 10 != 0) return;
        int chance = Math.min(70, 10 + pressure * 5);
        if (rng.nextInt(100) >= chance) return;
        String reason = "civil/noble-sector patrol sweep in " + world.zoneType.label + " with heat " + gangHeat + " and suspicion " + suspicion;
        lastArbitesPatrolReport = "Civic Wardens patrol initiates inspection: " + reason + ".";
        logEvent("CIVIC WARDENS PATROL: " + lastArbitesPatrolReport);
        handleInterrogation(Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS, reason);
    }
```

Name: handleArbitesCapture
SHA256: 84e12ef9db7d47f033866e2936c460e5961f53b455907a442ebeb583a12307fc

```java
    void handleArbitesCapture(String reason, int severity) {
        if (screen == Screen.LOST || active == null) return;
        severity = Math.max(1, Math.min(8, severity));
        int startTurn = turn;
        int startCarried = carriedScript;
        int startBanked = totalBankedCash();
        int startBaseStash = baseStashedScript;
        int baseFine = 35 + suspicion * 18 + gangHeat * 7 + severity * 45 + rng.nextInt(90 + severity * 30);
        int finePaid = payArbitesFine(baseFine);
        int unpaidFine = Math.max(0, baseFine - finePaid);
        int jailHours = Math.max(3, Math.min(72, 4 + severity * 3 + rng.nextInt(8 + severity * 4)));
        int statLosses = 1 + (severity >= 4 && rng.nextBoolean() ? 1 : 0);
        ArrayList<String> losses = new ArrayList<>();
        boolean fatalCustodyStatLoss = false;
        for (int i=0; i<statLosses; i++) {
            String loss = applyRandomArbitesStatLoss();
            losses.add(loss);
            if (loss.contains("FATAL CUSTODY TRAUMA")) fatalCustodyStatLoss = true;
        }
        int itemLoss = arbitesEvidenceItemLoss(severity);
        advancePlayerAndWorldTime(jailHours * TURNS_PER_HOUR, "Civic Wardens custody time");
        int fatigueBefore = fatigue, sleepBefore = sleepNeed, painBefore = pain, woundsBefore = wounds;
        fatigue = Math.min(30, fatigue + 4 + severity);
        sleepNeed = Math.min(MAX_SLEEP_NEED, sleepNeed + jailHours * TURNS_PER_HOUR / 2);
        pain = Math.min(24, pain + 2 + severity);
        wounds = Math.min(19, wounds + Math.max(1, severity / 2));
        suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - (4 + severity));
        temporaryHostileTurns.remove(Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS);
        arbitesCaptureCooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(arbitesCaptureCooldownUntilTurn, turn + ARBITES_CAPTURE_COOLDOWN_TURNS);
        arbitesInspectionCooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(arbitesInspectionCooldownUntilTurn, turn + ARBITES_INSPECTION_COOLDOWN_TURNS);
        int endBanked = totalBankedCash();
        lastCrimePunishmentReport = "Captured by Civic Wardens for " + reason + ". Hard time " + jailHours + "h, fine assessed " + baseFine + ", collected " + finePaid + ", stat loss " + String.join(", ", losses) + ", evidence items lost " + itemLoss + ".";
        ArrayList<String> detail = new ArrayList<>();
        detail.add("ADEPTUS CIVIC WARDENS CUSTODY REPORT");
        detail.add("Cause: " + reason + ".");
        detail.add("Severity: " + severity + " / 8.");
        detail.add("Time taken: " + jailHours + " local hour(s). Turn " + startTurn + " -> " + turn + ".");
        detail.add("Fine assessed: " + baseFine + " Concord Script. Paid/seized: " + finePaid + ". Unpaid docket remainder: " + unpaidFine + ".");
        detail.add("Carried script: " + startCarried + " -> " + carriedScript + ". Banked script: " + startBanked + " -> " + endBanked + ". Base stash: " + startBaseStash + " -> " + baseStashedScript + ".");
        detail.add("Items confiscated into evidence: " + itemLoss + ".");
        detail.add("Stat damage: " + (losses.isEmpty() ? "none" : String.join(", ", losses)) + ".");
        detail.add("Trauma: fatigue " + fatigueBefore + " -> " + fatigue + ", sleep debt " + sleepBefore + " -> " + sleepNeed + ", pain " + painBefore + " -> " + pain + ", wounds " + woundsBefore + " -> " + wounds + ".");
        detail.add("Street inspection cooldown until: " + TimeSurfaceApi.timeTextAtTurn(arbitesInspectionCooldownUntilTurn) + ".");
        detail.add("Fresh jail-processing cooldown until: " + TimeSurfaceApi.timeTextAtTurn(arbitesCaptureCooldownUntilTurn) + ".");
        if (fatalCustodyStatLoss) detail.add("Outcome: fatal custody trauma. A core stat reached zero.");
        else detail.add("Outcome: released from holding near an Civic Wardens authority point. The paperwork is not apology; it is inventory.");
        lastCustodyReportDetailed = String.join("\n", detail);
        lastInterrogation = lastCrimePunishmentReport;
        if (fatalCustodyStatLoss) {
            lastCrimePunishmentReport += " The beating reduced a core stat to zero; death in police custody recorded.";
            lastInterrogation = lastCrimePunishmentReport;
            lastCustodyReportDetailed += "\nFinal status: death in police custody.";
            logEvent("CIVIC WARDENS CUSTODY DEATH: " + lastCrimePunishmentReport);
            DebugLog.audit("ARBITES_CUSTODY_DEATH", lastCustodyReportDetailed.replace('\n',' ') + " state=" + stateSummary());
            triggerPlayerDeath("death in Civic Wardens police custody after repeated beatings", "Adeptus Civic Wardens custody", "institutional brutality", "precinct holding cell");
            return;
        }
        Point release = nearestArbitesReleasePoint();
        if (release != null) { playerX = release.x; playerY = release.y; lookX = playerX; lookY = playerY; }
        updateSensoryModel("Civic Wardens release");
        logEvent("CIVIC WARDENS CAPTURE: " + lastCrimePunishmentReport);
        DebugLog.audit("ARBITES_CAPTURE", lastCustodyReportDetailed.replace('\n',' ') + " state=" + stateSummary());
        maybeAutosave("Civic Wardens release");
        setScreen(Screen.CAPTURE);
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void talkToNpc(NpcEntity npc) {
        if (npc != null) runNpcTalkedTo++;
        activeConversationNpc = npc;
        selectedTradeOffer = 0;
        if (npc.isTrader()) {
            activeTrader = TraderSession.forNpc(npc, world == null ? ZoneType.NEUTRAL_CIVILIAN_FLOOR : world.zoneType, rng);
            activeTrader.sourceSite = siteForFaction(npc.faction, world == null ? ZoneType.NEUTRAL_CIVILIAN_FLOOR : world.zoneType);
            activeTrader.applyNpcSiteStock(activeTrader.sourceSite, rng, world, turn);
            activeTrader.applySupplyChainStock(world, turn, rng);
            conversationBranch = npc.name + ": I buy, I sell, and I remember faces. Try not to make yours expensive.";
            lastTradeReport = "Trader contacted: " + npc.name + " inventory=" + activeTrader.offers.size() + " zone=" + activeTrader.zoneLabel + ".";
            logConversation("OPEN_TRADER", conversationBranch);
            openPanel(PanelMode.TRADE);
            return;
        }
        activeTrader = null;
        if (npc.isProtectedCleric()) {
            conversationBranch = npc.name + ": The temple stands even when its congregation does not. Confess, pray, or leave your sins where the floor can count them.";
            lastConversation = conversationBranch;
            logConversation("MINISTORUM_HEAD_CLERIC", conversationBranch);
            openPanel(PanelMode.TRADE);
            return;
        }
        conversationBranch = npcGreeting(npc);
        lastConversation = npc.name + " says: " + conversationBranch;
        logConversation("NPC_TALK", npc.name + " faction=" + npc.faction.label + " state=" + npc.state + " role=" + npc.role + " line=" + conversationBranch);
        openPanel(PanelMode.TRADE);
    }
```

```java
    void listenToPortableBroadcastReceiver(String item) {
        String low = item == null ? "" : item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        String kind = low.contains("pict") || low.contains("screen") || low.contains("television") ? "pict-screen" : "radio";
        String report = ImperialNewsNetworkApi.broadcastBulletin(this, kind + "/portable", rng);
        lastBroadcastReport = report;
        lastInnNewsIssue = report;
        logEvent("PORTABLE INN " + kind.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + ": " + report);
        gainXp("Investigation", 1, "monitored portable INN broadcast");
        DebugLog.audit("INN_PORTABLE_BROADCAST", "item=" + item + " kind=" + kind + " report=" + report + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("listens to a carried broadcast receiver.");
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void takeSectorRailToNewSector() {
        if (!selectedInteractionIsSectorRail()) { logEvent("Sector rail failed: select a rail platform or depot counter inside a Neutral Rail Depot."); return; }
        int fare = sectorRailFare();
        if (!spendImperialScript(fare)) {
            logEvent("Sector rail blocked: passage to another sector costs " + fare + " Concord Script. You have " + countMoney() + ".");
            return;
        }
        int abandonedObjects = baseObjects.size();
        int abandonedRecruits = factionRecruits.size();
        int abandonedStorage = baseStorage.size();
        long oldSeed = seed;
        seed = mixNewSectorSeed(seed, turn, countMoney(), xp, knowledgeCredits);
        atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed);
        atlas.generateScaffold();
        atlas.sectorX = 1; atlas.sectorY = 1; atlas.zoneX = 2; atlas.zoneY = 2; atlas.floor = 5; atlas.sewer = false;
        baseClaimed = false; baseX = -1; baseY = -1; claimedRoomId = -1;
        baseObjects.clear(); baseStorage.clear(); factionRecruits.clear();
        gangHeat = Math.max(0, gangHeat / 4);
        suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion / 4);
        factionMarketPressure.clear(); initFactionState();
        visitedZoneInstances.clear(); visitedZoneTypes.clear();
        scavengeCooldownUntilTurn.clear();
        loadingForNewGame = false;
        loadingForTransition = true;
        loadingProgress = 0; loadingStep = 0; loadingStartMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
        lastLoadingPulseMillis = loadingStartMillis; loadingWatchdogReported = false; loadingWatchdogRepeats = 0;
        loadingStatus = "Taking sector rail to a new jurisdiction.";
        loadingDetail = "Abandoning local bases/recruits/storage; preserving carried inventory, body state, XP, and unlocked knowledge.";
        pendingTransitionReason = "sector rail relocation";
        pendingTransitionEdgeHint = null;
        pendingTransitionReturnEdge = "";
        logEvent("SECTOR RAIL: fare " + fare + " paid. Abandoned " + abandonedObjects + " base objects, " + abandonedRecruits + " recruits, and " + abandonedStorage + " stored goods. Carried items and knowledge remain.");
        DebugLog.audit("SECTOR_RAIL_DEPART", "oldSeed=" + oldSeed + " newSeed=" + seed + " fare=" + fare + " abandonedObjects=" + abandonedObjects + " abandonedRecruits=" + abandonedRecruits + " abandonedStorage=" + abandonedStorage + " state=" + stateSummary());
```

```java
    void completeAtlasWorldLoad(String reason, Point edgeHint) {
        try {
            World oldWorld = world;
            world = atlas.currentWorld();
            sanitizeCurrentWorldFeaturePlacement("transition currentWorld");
            spawnContractTargetsForCurrentWorld();
            boolean firstType = markZoneVisitedAndCheckFirstType();
            visibleTiles = new boolean[world.w][world.h];
            rememberedTiles = new boolean[world.w][world.h];
            localDirtyTracker.reset(world, "world-load");
            lastVisibilityDirtyRect = null;
            Point p = spawnPointForTransition(edgeHint);
            playerX = Math.max(1, Math.min(world.w - 2, p.x));
            playerY = Math.max(1, Math.min(world.h - 2, p.y));
            lookX = playerX; lookY = playerY; lookCursorActive = false; interactCursorActive = false;
            singlePlayerSectorBridge.bindCurrentWorld(this, "transition " + reason);
            openPanel(PanelMode.NONE);
            updateSensoryModel("transition " + reason);
            advanceTurn("travels by " + reason + ".");
            String event = maybeRollZoneTransitionEvent(reason);
            logEvent("Transition complete: " + reason + ". Now in sector " + atlas.sectorX + "," + atlas.sectorY + " zone " + atlas.zoneX + "," + atlas.zoneY + " floor " + atlas.floor + (atlas.sewer?"B sewer":"") + ".");
            if (event != null && !event.isEmpty()) logEvent(event);
            autosaveZoneTransition(reason);
            if (firstType) { prepareZoneSplash("new zone type discovered during transition"); setScreen(Screen.ZONE_SPLASH); }
            else setScreen(Screen.GAME);
            DebugLog.audit("ATLAS_TRANSITION", "reason="+reason+" old="+(oldWorld!=null?oldWorld.layerText():"none")+" new="+world.layerText()+" zone="+atlas.zoneX+","+atlas.zoneY+" firstType="+firstType+" event="+lastTransitionEvent+" player="+playerX+","+playerY+" state="+stateSummary());
        } catch (Throwable t) {
            DebugLog.error("ATLAS_TRANSITION_FAILED", "Failed to transition: " + reason, t);
            logEvent("ERROR: transition failed. Diagnostic details were recorded.");
            setScreen(Screen.GAME);
        }
    }
```

```java
    void talkToFactionRepresentative() {
        Faction f = nearestFactionForRepresentative();
        lastContractFaction = f;
        int standing = factionStanding.getOrDefault(f, 0);
        int bribeCost = Math.max(2, 4 - standing) + Math.max(0, -standing * 2);
        String board = contractBoardLine(f);
        if (supplies >= bribeCost && standing < 2) {
            supplies -= bribeCost;
            factionStanding.put(f, standing + 2);
            temporaryHostileTurns.put(f, 0);
            lastConversation = f.label + " representative accepted a bribe of " + bribeCost + " supplies. Standing improves to " + factionStanding.get(f) + ". " + board;
        } else if (standing >= 2) {
            lastConversation = f.label + " representative says you are currently useful enough to remain breathing. " + board;
        } else {
            lastConversation = f.label + " representative quotes a bribe of " + bribeCost + " supplies. You have " + supplies + ". Poverty is not a legal defense. " + board;
        }
        conversationBranch = lastConversation;
        activeTrader = null;
        activeConversationNpc = NpcEntity.factionRepresentative(f, playerX, playerY, rng);
        DebugLog.audit("FACTION_REP", lastConversation + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent(lastConversation);
        openPanel(PanelMode.TRADE);
    }
```

```java
    void startGame() {
        DebugLog.audit("START_GAME", "candidateIndex=" + candidateIndex + " jobIndex=" + jobIndex + " candidates=" + candidates.size());
        Candidate sourceCandidate = candidates.get(candidateIndex);
        sourceCandidate.name = CharacterCreationAuthority.sanitizePlayerName(sourceCandidate.name, rng);
        refreshNameLockedCandidateState(sourceCandidate);
        characterNameEditActive = false;
        JobProfile chosenJob = JobProfile.get(sourceCandidate.jobs.get(jobIndex));
        if (!chosenJob.meets(sourceCandidate)) {
            logEvent("Invalid job: " + chosenJob.name + " requires " + chosenJob.requirementText() + ". Roll another character or choose another occupation.");
            DebugLog.audit("START_BLOCKED_INVALID_JOB", "candidate=" + sourceCandidate.name + " job=" + chosenJob.name + " missing=" + chosenJob.missingText(sourceCandidate));
            return;
        }
        pendingStartCandidate = sourceCandidate.copy();
        pendingStartJob = chosenJob;
        loadingSeed = worldSelectedForCharacter ? seed : (System.currentTimeMillis() ^ pendingStartCandidate.name.hashCode() ^ chosenJob.name.hashCode());
        loadingProgress = 0; loadingStep = 0; loadingForNewGame = true; loadingStartMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
        lastLoadingPulseMillis = loadingStartMillis; loadingWatchdogReported = false; loadingWatchdogRepeats = 0; loadingFinalizationStarted = false; loadingFinalizationRunning = false; loadingFinalizationKind = "new-game";
        loadingStatus = "Igniting sector cartograph engine.";
        loadingDetail = "Queued: world seed, runtime settings, sector atlas, faction ledgers, and player insertion state.";
        setScreen(Screen.LOADING);
        ensureRuntimeTimerRunning("new-game loading");
        DebugLog.audit("LOADING_BEGIN", "newGame=true seed=" + loadingSeed + " job=" + chosenJob.name + " timerRunning=" + timer.isRunning());
    }
```

Name: progressLoading
SHA256: a4a6460e3b54bd267e76809c700f9ff6f73e173641939489073ade762b5e77a6

```java
    void progressLoading() {
        if (screen != Screen.LOADING) return;
        lastLoadingPulseMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
        if (loadingFinalizationStarted) {
            loadingProgress = Math.max(96, Math.min(99, loadingProgress + (loadingFinalizationRunning ? 0 : 1)));
            return;
        }
        loadingStep++;
        String[] statuses = {
            "Reading project files and runtime settings.",
            "Generating current sector atlas.",
            "Creating active zone room/corridor graph.",
            "Validating doors, sewers, elevators, and edge transitions.",
            "Assigning faction claims and room service roles.",
            "Indexing scavenge ledgers, infopedia labels, and map descriptors.",
            "Allocating fog-of-war, sensory, and player state buffers.",
            "Finalizing player insertion room pointer."
        };
        String[] details = {
            "Files: settings/options.properties; assets/generated/the_mechanist_title.png; imported GUI/button sprites; docs generation references.",
            "Process: WorldAtlas.generateScaffold() builds active slice now; provenance-aware full-sector pregen remains lazy/runtime bounded.",
            "Process: atlas.currentWorld() resolves the active zone and confirms structured hab/sewer room templates.",
            "Process: edge doors, hatch/ladder links, elevator caps, and transition spawn hints are being checked.",
            "Process: zone type doctrine assigns gangs, Civic Wardens, Mechanist Collegia, civilians, sewer camps, or service-spine control.",
            "Process: room descriptors, scavenge tables, shop/vending hooks, and Infopedia zone names are being indexed.",
            "Process: visibleTiles, rememberedTiles, sense pings, event log state, and panel caches are being prepared.",
            "Process: world.startPoint()/ensurePlayerSpawnPoint() must return a walkable tile with a valid room id."
        };
        int beforeProgress = loadingProgress;
        loadingProgress = Math.min(96, loadingProgress + 7 + (loadingStep % 4));
        int statusIndex = Math.min(statuses.length-1, loadingStep / 3);
        loadingStatus = statuses[statusIndex];
        loadingDetail = details[statusIndex];
        if (loadingStep == 1 || loadingProgress / 20 != beforeProgress / 20 || loadingProgress >= 96) {
            DebugLog.audit("LOADING_PROGRESS", "step=" + loadingStep + " progress=" + loadingProgress + " status=" + loadingStatus + " detail=" + loadingDetail);
        }
        if ((loadingProgress >= 96 || loadingStep > 24) && System.currentTimeMillis() - loadingStartMillis >= 1400) {
            startLoadingFinalizationWorker(loadingForTransition ? "transition" : "new-game");
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:3645-3673
Kind: method
Name: startLoadingFinalizationWorker
SHA256: 2d4a72b2bdd02ce8041b1637b9eba9aa5ef8fd43458536299deb179b3e3612e8

```java
    void startLoadingFinalizationWorker(String kind) {
        if (loadingFinalizationStarted) return;
        loadingFinalizationStarted = true;
        loadingFinalizationRunning = true;
        loadingFinalizationStartMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
        loadingFinalizationKind = kind == null ? "unknown" : kind;
        loadingStatus = "Finalizing " + loadingFinalizationKind + " runtime state.";
        loadingDetail = "Finalizer substeps will report atlas, world, player, sensory, and insertion work separately.";
        loadingProgress = Math.max(96, loadingProgress);
        DebugLog.audit("LOADING_FINALIZER_BEGIN", "kind=" + loadingFinalizationKind + " step=" + loadingStep + " progress=" + loadingProgress + " state=" + stateSummary());
        Thread t = new Thread(() -> {
            try {
                if (loadingForTransition) finishLoadingTransition();
                else finishLoadingNewGame();
            } catch (Throwable ex) {
                DebugLog.error("LOADING_FINALIZER_THREAD_FAILED", "Background loading finalizer crashed kind=" + loadingFinalizationKind, ex);
                SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
                    loadingStatus = "Loader failed; returned to main menu.";
                    loadingDetail = "Diagnostic details were recorded. The background finalizer trapped a hard fault instead of freezing at zero.";
                    setScreen(Screen.MENU);
                });
            } finally {
                loadingFinalizationRunning = false;
                DebugLog.audit("LOADING_FINALIZER_END", "kind=" + loadingFinalizationKind + " elapsedMs=" + (System.currentTimeMillis() - loadingFinalizationStartMillis));
            }
        }, "mechanist-loading-finalizer");
        t.setDaemon(true);
        t.start();
    }
```

```java
    void finishLoadingTransition() {
        try {
            completeAtlasWorldLoad(pendingTransitionReason, pendingTransitionEdgeHint);
            loadingForTransition = false;
            pendingTransitionReason = "";
            pendingTransitionEdgeHint = null;
            pendingTransitionReturnEdge = "";
        } catch (Throwable t) {
            loadingForTransition = false;
            DebugLog.error("LOADING_TRANSITION_FAILED", "Could not finish map transition.", t);
            logEvent("ERROR: transition loading failed. Diagnostic details were recorded.");
            setScreen(Screen.GAME);
        }
    }
```

```java
    void finishLoadingNewGame() {
        try {
            updateLoadingPhase("Finalizer 1/8: binding selected character.", "Copying candidate, job, and selected world setup into the new runtime envelope.", 96);
            Candidate sourceCandidate = pendingStartCandidate;
            JobProfile chosenJob = pendingStartJob;
            active = sourceCandidate.copy();
            AgeAndWorldTimeAuthority.synchronizeCandidate(active, worldTurn);
            active.job = chosenJob.name;
            seed = loadingSeed;
            updateLoadingPhase("Finalizer 2/8: preparing sector atlas.", "Resolving seed, world profile, and atlas scaffold before selecting the current zone.", 96);
            NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.setActiveOperatorProfileName(resolveOperatorProfileName());
            if (atlas == null || atlas.seed != seed) atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed, worldSetup);
            WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(worldSetup);
            atlas.generateScaffold();
            updateLoadingPhase("Finalizer 3/8: loading current zone.", "Fetching the current world slice, repairing feature placement, and spawning contracts.", 97);
            world = atlas.currentWorld();
            sanitizeCurrentWorldFeaturePlacement("new game currentWorld");
            spawnContractTargetsForCurrentWorld();

            rememberedTiles = new boolean[world.w][world.h];
            Point p = world.startPoint();
            playerX = p.x; playerY = p.y;
            if (world.roomIdAt(playerX, playerY) < 0 || !world.walkable(playerX, playerY)) {
                Point safe = world.ensurePlayerSpawnPoint();
                playerX = safe.x; playerY = safe.y;
```

```java
    @Override protected void paintComponent(Graphics g0) {
        long start = System.nanoTime();
        try {
            int physicalW = Math.max(1, super.getWidth());
            int physicalH = Math.max(1, super.getHeight());
            boolean readableUiPass = screen != Screen.GAME;
            BufferedImage buffer = renderScaling.ensureInternalBuffer(readableUiPass);
            Graphics2D g = buffer.createGraphics();
            try {
                g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.Src);
                g.setColor(Color.BLACK);
                g.fillRect(0, 0, buffer.getWidth(), buffer.getHeight());
                g.setComposite(AlphaComposite.SrcOver);
                DisplayDensityAuthority.applyTextRenderingHints(g, options);
                VisualJuiceFramework.applyHighQualityHints(g);
                DisplayDensityAuthority.applyTextRenderingHints(g, options);
                g.scale(renderScaling.bufferScaleX(readableUiPass), renderScaling.bufferScaleY(readableUiPass));
                virtualRenderContext = true;
                renderGameSurface(g);
                AccessibilityCompatibilityAuthority.processCompositedBackbuffer(buffer, options);
                if (singlePlayerSectorBridge != null) singlePlayerSectorBridge.noteSnapshotRendered("paintComponent");
            } finally {
                virtualRenderContext = false;
                g.dispose();
            }

            Graphics2D screen = (Graphics2D)g0.create();
            try {
                screen.setColor(Color.BLACK);
                screen.fillRect(0, 0, physicalW, physicalH);
                RenderScalingCrtAuthority.Layout layout = renderScaling.layoutFor(physicalW, physicalH);
                DisplayDensityAuthority.applyTextRenderingHints(screen, options);
                VisualJuiceFramework.applyGpuFriendlyHints(screen);
                DisplayDensityAuthority.applyTextRenderingHints(screen, options);
                screen.setRenderingHint(RenderingHints.KEY_INTERPOLATION, readableUiPass ? RenderingHints.VALUE_INTERPOLATION_NEAREST_NEIGHBOR : RenderingHints.VALUE_INTERPOLATION_BILINEAR);
                screen.drawImage(buffer, layout.x, layout.y, layout.width, layout.height, null);
                if (renderScaling.profile().crtEnabled) {
                    screen.drawImage(renderScaling.ensureCrtOverlay(layout.width, layout.height), layout.x, layout.y, null);
                }
                long overlayElapsed = System.nanoTime() - start;
                performanceDiagnostics.recordFrame(overlayElapsed);
                frameLimiter.recordFrame(overlayElapsed, renderStressTest.activeElements());
                performanceDiagnostics.draw(screen, this, physicalW, physicalH);
                if (options.diagnosticsOverlay || renderStressTest.active()) frameLimiter.drawOverlay(screen, physicalW, physicalH, renderStressTest.active());
            } finally {
                screen.dispose();
            }

            long elapsed = System.nanoTime() - start;
            frameCount++;
            if (elapsed > worstFrameNanos) worstFrameNanos = elapsed;
            if (frameCount % 300 == 0) {
                String metric = "Benchmark frame=" + frameCount + " worstPaintMs=" + String.format(Locale.US, "%.3f", worstFrameNanos/1_000_000.0)
                        + " renderProfile=" + renderScaling.profileLabel() + " internal=" + renderScaling.internalWidth() + "x" + renderScaling.internalHeight()
                        + " scaledImageCache=" + RenderImageScaleCacheAuthority.cacheSize()
                        + " textWrapCache=" + TextLayoutAuthority.cacheSize();
                logEvent(metric);
                DebugLog.metric("paint", metric + " | " + stateSummary());
            }
        } catch (Throwable t) {
            virtualRenderContext = false;
            DebugLog.error("PAINT", "paintComponent failed | state=" + stateSummary(), t);
            try {
                g0.setColor(Color.BLACK); g0.fillRect(0,0,Math.max(1, super.getWidth()),Math.max(1, super.getHeight()));
                g0.setColor(Color.RED); DisplayDensityAuthority.applyTinyTextRenderingHints((Graphics2D)g0); g0.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, 16));
                g0.drawString("RENDER ERROR - diagnostic details recorded", 32, 64);
            } catch (Throwable ignored) {}
        }
    }

```

```java
    void renderGameSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        drawBackground(g);
        scrollRegions.clear();
        rebuildButtons();
        clampButtonsToVisibleMenuBounds();
        applySemanticButtonIcons();
        assignButtonDebugIds();
        if (screen == Screen.BOOT) drawBoot(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.LOADING) drawLoading(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.MENU) drawMenu(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.MODS) drawModsSurface(g);
            else if (screen == Screen.EDITOR) drawInGameEditorSurface(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.MULTIPLAYER) drawMultiplayerSurface(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) drawSectorAuditSurface(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SELECT) drawWorldSelect(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP) drawWorldSetup(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.CHARACTER) drawCharacter(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.KNOWLEDGE) drawKnowledgeScreen(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) drawIntroCrawl(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.GAME) {
            drawGame(g);
            renderNormalModeVisualJuice(g);
            firstPersonRenderViewport.render(g, this);
        }
        else if (screen == Screen.PAUSE) drawPause(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.PANEL) drawPanel(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.ZONE_SPLASH) drawZoneSplash(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.CAPTURE) drawCaptureScreen(g);
        else if (screen == Screen.LOST) drawLostScreen(g);
        else drawOptions(g);
        if (options.screenSaver && screen != Screen.BOOT && screen != Screen.LOADING && System.currentTimeMillis() - lastInputMillis > 15L*60L*1000L) drawIdleScreensaver(g);
        if (eulaGateActive) drawEulaOverlay(g);
        int hoverButtonIndex = activeHoverButtonIndex();
        for (int i=0;i<buttons.size();i++) buttons.get(i).draw(g, uiFont, i==selectedButton || i==hoverButtonIndex, images, options);
        drawHoverHelp(g, hoverButtonIndex);
        // Modal/profile/info alerts must sit above menu buttons, not beneath them.
        drawTimedAlert(g);
    }
```

```java
    Runnable launcherMenuAction(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route route) {
        LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route safeRoute = route == null ? LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.START : route;
        switch (safeRoute) {
            case START: return this::openWorldSelection;
            case LOAD_AUTO: return () -> { launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.LOAD_AUTO, "main menu load/save"); openPanel(PanelMode.SAVELOAD); };
            case OPTIONS: return () -> { launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.OPTIONS, "main menu options"); setScreen(Screen.OPTIONS); };
            case EXIT: return () -> { launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.EXIT, "main menu exit"); System.exit(0); };
            case MODS: return this::openModsLauncherSurface;
            case MULTIPLAYER: return this::openMultiplayerLauncherSurface;
            case INFOPEDIA: return () -> { launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.INFOPEDIA, "main menu infopedia"); openPanel(PanelMode.INFOPEDIA); };
            case PROFILE: return this::openUserProfileSurface;
            default: return this::openWorldSelection;
        }
    }
```

```java
    void openWorldSelection() {
        logEvent(launcherShell.activate(LauncherShellStateAuthority.Route.START, "main menu start"));
        logEvent(launcherRuntime.prepareLocalServer("main menu start"));
        availableWorlds = WorldSaveInfo.listExistingWorlds();
        selectedWorldIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, Math.max(0, availableWorlds.size()-1)));
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            pendingWorldSetup = WorldSetupSettings.standard();
            lastWorldSetupReport = "No saved world definitions found. Configure and generate a new arcology world first.";
            setScreen(Screen.WORLD_SETUP);
        } else {
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Found " + availableWorlds.size() + " saved world definition(s). Select one or generate a new world.";
            setScreen(Screen.WORLD_SELECT);
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:31-45

```java
    void useSelectedWorldForCharacterCreation() {
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) { openWorldSelection(); return; }
        WorldSaveInfo info = availableWorlds.get(Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, availableWorlds.size()-1)));
        seed = info.seed;
        worldSetup = info.settings.copy();
        WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(worldSetup);
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.setActiveOperatorProfileName(resolveOperatorProfileName());
        atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed, worldSetup);
        worldSelectedForCharacter = true;
        selectedWorldSummary = info.summaryLine();
        generateCandidates(); candidateIndex = 0; jobIndex = 0; jobDossierScroll = 0; jobDossierTab = 0;
        logEvent("WORLD SELECTED: " + selectedWorldSummary);
        DebugLog.audit("WORLD_SELECTED_FOR_CHARACTER", selectedWorldSummary);
        setScreen(Screen.CHARACTER);
    }
```

```java
    void generateConfiguredWorldForCharacterCreation() {
        worldSetup = pendingWorldSetup == null ? WorldSetupSettings.standard() : pendingWorldSetup.copy();
        WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(worldSetup);
        seed = System.currentTimeMillis() ^ Objects.hash(worldSetup.encode(), availableWorlds.size(), eventLog.size());
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.setActiveOperatorProfileName(resolveOperatorProfileName());
        atlas = new WorldAtlas(seed, worldSetup);
        worldSelectedForCharacter = true;
        selectedWorldSummary = atlas.hiveWorld.summary();
        lastWorldSetupReport = "Generated " + selectedWorldSummary;
        generateCandidates(); candidateIndex = 0; jobIndex = 0; jobDossierScroll = 0; jobDossierTab = 0;
        logEvent("WORLD GENERATED: " + selectedWorldSummary);
        DebugLog.audit("WORLD_GENERATED_FOR_CHARACTER", selectedWorldSummary + " setup=" + worldSetup.encode());
        setScreen(Screen.CHARACTER);
    }
```

```java
    Rectangle mainMenuSubtitleRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        int cx = W / 2;
        BufferedImage title = images.get("title_mechanist_rebase");
        if (title == null) title = images.get("title_mechanist");
        int titleTop = mainMenuTitleTop(H);
        int drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + 112;
        if (title != null) {
            Dimension titleSize = mainMenuTitleDrawSize(title, W, H);
            drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + titleSize.height;
        }
        BufferedImage subtitle = images.get("subtitle_rebase");
        if (subtitle == null) return new Rectangle(cx - 360, drawnTitleBottom + 3, 720, 74);
        Dimension subSize = mainMenuSubtitleDrawSize(subtitle, W, H);
        int sy = drawnTitleBottom + 3;
        return new Rectangle(cx - subSize.width / 2, sy, subSize.width, subSize.height);
    }
```

```java
    Rectangle mainMenuButtonFrameRect() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        Rectangle subtitle = mainMenuSubtitleRect();
        int frameW = Math.max(520, Math.min(subtitle.width, W - 120));
        int minY = subtitle.y + subtitle.height + 8;
        int runtimeReserveTop = H - Math.max(70, Math.min(96, H / 10));
        int availableH = runtimeReserveTop - minY;
        // 0.9.10ip: prefer a taller launcher bay so six route buttons plus EXIT get
        // discrete rows. If the splash stack consumes too much space, reclaim from the bottom
        // first before allowing the route frame to collapse.
        int desiredH = Math.max(142, Math.min(196, H / 5));
        int frameH = Math.max(128, Math.min(desiredH, availableH - 4));
        int y = minY;
        if (availableH < 136) {
            frameH = Math.max(118, Math.min(154, runtimeReserveTop - subtitle.y - subtitle.height - 4));
            y = Math.max(subtitle.y + subtitle.height + 4, runtimeReserveTop - frameH);
        }
        return new Rectangle((W - frameW) / 2, y, frameW, frameH);
    }
```

```java
    void rebuildInGameEditorButtons() {
        Rectangle outer = inGameEditorOuterRect();
        Rectangle tabs = inGameEditorTabRect();
        Rectangle left = inGameEditorLeftRect();
        Rectangle right = inGameEditorRightRect();
        int gap = Math.max(5, scaled(5));
        java.util.List<String> names = inGameEditorNames();
        int tabW = Math.max(84, (tabs.width - gap * Math.max(0, names.size()-1)) / Math.max(1, names.size()));
        for (int i=0;i<names.size();i++) {
            final int idx = i;
            String label = (i == inGameEditorTabIndex ? "▶ " : "") + names.get(i).replace(" Editor", "").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(label, tabs.x + i*(tabW+gap), tabs.y, tabW, tabs.height, "Switch to " + names.get(i) + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorTab(idx)));
        }
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("BACK", outer.x + 18, outer.y + 14, 110, 30, "Return to Mods / Tools.", () -> setScreen(Screen.MODS)));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("NEW " + inGameEditorName().replace(" Editor", "").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT), left.x + 12, left.y + 36, left.width - 24, 28, "Create a fresh blank entry for the active editor.", this::createNewInGameEditorEntry));
        java.util.List<SimulationEditorRepository.EditableEntity> entities = inGameEditorEntities();
        int rowH = Math.max(24, Math.min(30, (left.height - 92) / Math.max(4, Math.min(10, Math.max(1, entities.size())))));
        int listY = left.y + 76;
        int visible = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, (left.y + left.height - listY - 12) / Math.max(1, rowH)));
        for (int i=0;i<Math.min(visible, entities.size());i++) {
            final int idx = i;
            String label = (i == inGameEditorEntityIndex ? "▶ " : "") + entities.get(i).name();
            buttons.add(new ButtonBox(label, left.x + 12, listY + i*rowH, left.width - 24, rowH - 3, "Select editor record " + entities.get(i).id() + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorEntity(idx)));
        }
        int cmdX = right.x + 12;
        int cmdW = right.width - 24;
        int y = right.y + right.height - 112;
        int bw = Math.max(86, (cmdW - gap) / 2);
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("UNDO", cmdX, y, bw, 26, "Undo the last editor command.", this::inGameEditorUndo));
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("REDO", cmdX + bw + gap, y, bw, 26, "Redo the last editor command.", this::inGameEditorRedo));
        y += 32;
        buttons.add(new ButtonBox("HELP " + (inGameEditorHelpVisible ? "ON" : "OFF"), cmdX, y, cmdW, 26, "Show or hide the editor explanation banner.", () -> { inGameEditorHelpVisible = !inGameEditorHelpVisible; repaint(); }));
        if ("Room Editor".equals(inGameEditorName())) {
            String[][] p = inGameEditorPalettes();
            int py = right.y + 38;
            int catH = 24;
            for (int i=0;i<p.length;i++) {
                final int idx = i;
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox((i == inGameEditorPaletteTab ? "▶ " : "") + p[i][0], cmdX, py + i*(catH+3), cmdW, catH, "Choose room-editor palette category " + p[i][0] + ".", () -> selectInGameEditorPaletteTab(idx)));
            }
            int itemY = py + p.length*(catH+3) + 10;
            int itemH = 23;
            String[] active = p[Math.max(0, Math.min(p.length-1, inGameEditorPaletteTab))];
            for (int i=1; i<active.length && i<=8; i++) {
                final int idx = i - 1;
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox((idx == inGameEditorPaletteIndex ? "▶ " : "") + active[i], cmdX, itemY + idx*(itemH+3), cmdW, itemH, "Select palette item; left-click grid to place, right-click to erase.", () -> selectInGameEditorPaletteItem(idx)));
            }
        }
    }
```

```java
    void drawInGameEditorSurface(Graphics2D g) {

        Rectangle tabs = inGameEditorTabRect();
        Rectangle left = inGameEditorLeftRect();

            g.setFont(smallFont);

            drawInGameRoomEditor(g, entity, center);

            drawInGameGenericEditor(g, entity, center);
        }
        drawInGameEditorInspector(g, entity, right);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,170));
        g.fillRoundRect(status.x, status.y, status.width, status.height, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(new Color(130,112,70,150));

    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:939-953
Kind: method
Name: zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect
SHA256: 5017b9d83f2904bde7b5dabe4dd9f88e79b7277181591a735134c5be3a7fcc94

```java
    Rectangle zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect(UiLayout L) {
        if (L == null) L = uiLayout();
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        int screenPad = Math.max(8, scaled(8));
        int cols = zones.length > 14 ? 2 : 1;
        int rowH = Math.max(22, Math.min(28, L.command.height / 24));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (int)Math.ceil(zones.length / (double)Math.max(1, cols)));
        int w = Math.min(Math.max(360, getWidth() - screenPad * 2), Math.max(300, cols * 190 + 36));
        int h = Math.min(Math.max(160, L.command.height - 18), Math.max(110, 20 + rows * rowH + Math.max(0, rows - 1) * 4));
        int x = Math.max(screenPad, L.command.x - w - 10);
        if (x + w > getWidth() - screenPad) x = Math.max(screenPad, getWidth() - screenPad - w);
        int y = Math.max(screenPad, L.command.y + 10);
        if (y + h > getHeight() - screenPad) y = Math.max(screenPad, getHeight() - screenPad - h);
        return new Rectangle(x, y, w, h);
    }
```

SHA256: be7cafe68d475a30140ab35ece1c46032dc4c075dddaf80addbce7b29926150a

```java
    boolean isZoneAuditDropdownButton(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null || b.label == null || !auditZoneDropdownOpen || screen != Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) return false;
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        String label = b.label.replace("▶", "").trim();
        for (ZoneType z : zones) if (label.equals(z.label)) return true;
        return false;
    }
```

```java
    void drawSectorAuditZoneDropdown(Graphics2D g, UiLayout L) {
        if (!auditZoneDropdownOpen || L == null) return;
        ZoneType[] zones = ZoneType.values();
        if (zones.length == 0) return;
        Rectangle outer = zoneAuditDropdownOuterRect(L);
        Rectangle inner = zoneAuditDropdownInnerRect(L);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,232));
        g.fillRoundRect(outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height, 10, 10);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-zone-selector", outer.x, outer.y, outer.width, outer.height);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int colGap = Math.max(6, Math.min(10, inner.width / 38));
        int rowGap = Math.max(3, Math.min(5, inner.height / 80));
        int cols = Math.max(1, Math.min(3, (inner.width + colGap) / 170));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (int)Math.ceil(zones.length / (double)cols));
        int cellW = Math.max(120, (inner.width - colGap * Math.max(0, cols - 1)) / cols);
        int cellH = Math.max(18, Math.min(25, (inner.height - rowGap * Math.max(0, rows - 1)) / rows));
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(outer.x + 6, outer.y + 6, outer.width - 12, outer.height - 12);
        for (int i = 0; i < zones.length; i++) {
            int col = i % cols;
            int row = i / cols;
            int x = inner.x + col * (cellW + colGap);
            int y = inner.y + row * (cellH + rowGap);
            ZoneType z = zones[i];
            boolean selected = i == auditZoneTypeIndex;
            g.setColor(selected ? new Color(60,48,24,235) : new Color(10,10,10,188));
            g.fillRoundRect(x, y, cellW, cellH, 6, 6);
            g.setColor(selected ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel((selected ? "▶ " : "") + z.label, fm, cellW - 10), x + 6, y + Math.max(13, fm.getAscent() + 2));
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
    }
```

```java
    void drawSectorAuditInfoPanel(Graphics2D g, UiLayout L) {
        Rectangle t = L.tactical;
        g.setColor(new Color(6,7,7,238));
        g.fillRect(t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-report", t.x, t.y, t.width, t.height);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(9f, smallFont.getSize2D()-2f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "ZONE AUDIT REPORT", t.x + 12, t.y + 20);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (auditWorld == null) lines.add("No audit world generated.");
        else {
            char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(auditCursorX, auditCursorY) ? auditWorld.tiles[auditCursorX][auditCursorY] : '?';
            CompiledTileDescriptor d = TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(auditWorld, auditCursorX, auditCursorY, ch);
            lines.add("Zone: " + auditWorld.zoneType.label + " | " + auditWorld.w + "x" + auditWorld.h + " | weight " + WorldGenerationApi.worldgenWeightBandLabel(auditZoneSizeIndex) + " | density " + WorldSetupSettings.ZONE_DENSITY[Math.max(0, Math.min(3, auditZoneDensityIndex))] + " | overlay " + SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.overlayLabel(auditOverlayMode) + ".");
            SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.Step step = currentAuditTraceStep();
            if (step != null) lines.add(step.line(auditTraceSteps == null ? 0 : auditTraceSteps.size()) + (auditTracePlaying ? " | playing." : " | paused."));
            lines.add("Cursor: " + auditCursorX + "," + auditCursorY + " glyph '" + ch + "' room " + auditWorld.roomIdAt(auditCursorX, auditCursorY) + " faction " + auditWorld.roomFaction(auditWorld.roomIdAt(auditCursorX, auditCursorY)).label + ".");
            if (d != null) lines.add("Tile descriptor: " + d.inspectLine() + ".");
            lines.addAll(auditTileInspectionLines(auditCursorX, auditCursorY));
            lines.addAll(SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.compactPanelLines(auditSnapshot, auditFindingIndex));
            lines.add(auditReport);
        }
        int y = t.y + 42;
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(t.x + 8, t.y + 28, t.width - 16, t.height - 36);
        FontMetrics reportMetrics = g.getFontMetrics();
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap(String.join(" ", lines), Math.max(54, (t.width - 24) / Math.max(6, reportMetrics.charWidth('W'))))) {
            if (y > t.y + t.height - 8) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, line, t.x + 12, y);
            y += Math.max(12, reportMetrics.getHeight() + 1);
        }
        g.setClip(old);
    }
```

```java
    Rectangle multiplayerContentRect(Rectangle panel) {
```
