```java
    void REPLACED_OLD_DRAWMENU(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        BufferedImage title = images.get("title_mechanist_rebase");
        if (title == null) title = images.get("title_mechanist");
        int cx = W/2;
        int titleTop = mainMenuTitleTop(H);
        int drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + 112;
        if (title != null) {
            Dimension titleSize = mainMenuTitleDrawSize(title, W, H);
            int tw = titleSize.width;
            int th = titleSize.height;
            g.drawImage(title, cx-tw/2, titleTop, tw, th, null);
            stampUiFrameId(g, "I", "title-mechanist", cx-tw/2, titleTop, tw, th);
            drawnTitleBottom = titleTop + th;
        } else {
            g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(34f, Math.min(56f, H / 9f)))); g.setColor(new Color(200,184,132));
            center(g, "THE MECHANIST", cx, titleTop + 68);
        }
        BufferedImage subtitle = images.get("subtitle_rebase");
        int subtitleBottom = drawnTitleBottom + 6;
        if (subtitle != null) {
            Dimension subSize = mainMenuSubtitleDrawSize(subtitle, W, H);
            int sw = subSize.width;
            int sh = subSize.height;
            int sy = drawnTitleBottom + 3;
            g.drawImage(subtitle, cx-sw/2, sy, sw, sh, null);
            stampUiFrameId(g, "I", "subtitle", cx-sw/2, sy, sw, sh);
            subtitleBottom = sy + sh;
        }
        // No flavor blurb between title art and launcher buttons; title/splash art owns this space.
        Rectangle buttonFrame = mainMenuButtonFrameRect();

        g.fillRoundRect(buttonFrame.x, buttonFrame.y, buttonFrame.width, buttonFrame.height, 14, 14);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, buttonFrame.x, buttonFrame.y, buttonFrame.width, buttonFrame.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "main-menu-route-frame", buttonFrame.x, buttonFrame.y, buttonFrame.width, buttonFrame.height);
        java.util.List<String> shellLines = launcherShell.displayLines(launcherRuntime, userProfile);
        int panelW = Math.min(W - 220, 245);
        int panelH = Math.max(22, Math.min(26, H / 24));
        int panelX = (W - panelW) / 2;
        int panelY = H - panelH - 38;

        g.fillRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 9, 9);
        g.setColor(new Color(130,105,55,150));

        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();

        int maxLines = Math.max(1, (panelH - 8) / Math.max(10, fm.getHeight()));
        for (int i=0; i<shellLines.size() && i<maxLines; i++) {
            g.setColor(i == 0 ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(shellLines.get(i), fm, panelW - 20), cx, lineY);
            lineY += Math.max(10, fm.getHeight());
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
    }
```

```java
    void REPLACED_OLD_INTRO_CRAWL(Graphics2D g) {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        long elapsed = Math.max(0L, System.currentTimeMillis() - introCrawlStartMillis);
        BufferedImage backdrop = images.get("new_world_backdrop_rebase");
        if (backdrop != null) {
            double scale = Math.max(W / (double)Math.max(1, backdrop.getWidth()), H / (double)Math.max(1, backdrop.getHeight()));
            int bw = Math.max(W, (int)Math.round(backdrop.getWidth() * scale));
            int bh = Math.max(H, (int)Math.round(backdrop.getHeight() * scale));
            g.drawImage(backdrop, (W-bw)/2, (H-bh)/2, bw, bh, null);
        } else {
            g.setColor(new Color(5, 6, 8)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        }
        drawIntroCloudLayer(g, images.get("clouds_slow_rebase"), elapsed, 0.012, 34, 0.48f);
        drawIntroCloudLayer(g, images.get("clouds_fast_rebase"), elapsed, 0.026, 0, 0.38f);
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,126)); g.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 26, 26, W-52, H-52, "outer");

        int panelW = Math.min(Math.max(520, W - 240), W - 130);
        int panelX = (W - panelW) / 2;
        int panelY = Math.max(96, H / 5);
        int panelH = Math.max(280, H - panelY - 86);
        g.setColor(new Color(5,7,7,186)); g.fillRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 18, 18);
        g.setColor(new Color(156,132,78,190)); g.drawRoundRect(panelX, panelY, panelW, panelH, 18, 18);

        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(26f, Math.min(42f, H / 14f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE));
        center(g, "NEW WORLD INSERTION", W/2, Math.max(60, panelY - 44));
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(11f, Math.min(15f, H / 48f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        center(g, active == null ? "Unnamed operator" : active.name + " // " + active.job, W/2, Math.max(82, panelY - 18));

        if (introCrawlLines.isEmpty()) introCrawlLines = images.loadIntroCrawlLines();
        Font crawlFont = smallFont.deriveFont(Font.PLAIN, Math.max(13f, Math.min(17f, H / 42f)));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics(crawlFont);
        ArrayList<String> wrapped = new ArrayList<>();
        int wrapChars = Math.max(38, (panelW - 84) / Math.max(7, fm.charWidth('M')));
        for (String line : introCrawlLines) {
            String cleaned = line == null ? "" : line.trim();
            if (cleaned.isEmpty()) { wrapped.add(""); continue; }
            wrapped.addAll(TextSurfaceApi.wrap(cleaned, wrapChars));
            wrapped.add("");
        }
        while (!wrapped.isEmpty() && wrapped.get(wrapped.size()-1).isEmpty()) wrapped.remove(wrapped.size()-1);
        if (wrapped.isEmpty()) wrapped.add("The arcology opens beneath you.");

        final long leadInMs = 900L;
        final long blankMs = 760L;
        final long linePauseMs = 460L;
        final long charMs = introCrawlCharMillisForTarget(wrapped, leadInMs, blankMs, linePauseMs, INTRO_CRAWL_TEXT_TARGET_MS);
        int lineH = Math.max(24, fm.getHeight() + 8);
        long t = Math.max(0L, elapsed - leadInMs);
        long cursor = 0L;
        int currentLine = 0;
        int visibleChars = 0;
        float liftFraction = 0f;
        boolean finished = false;
        for (int i = 0; i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            long typeMs = line.isEmpty() ? blankMs : Math.max(780L, line.length() * charMs);
            if (t < cursor) {
                currentLine = Math.max(0, i - 1);
                visibleChars = wrapped.get(currentLine).length();
                liftFraction = 0f;
                break;
            }
            if (t < cursor + typeMs) {
                currentLine = i;
                if (line.isEmpty()) visibleChars = 0;
                else if (options.instantDialogueText) visibleChars = line.length();
                else visibleChars = Math.max(0, Math.min(line.length(), (int)((t - cursor) / Math.max(1L, charMs))));
                liftFraction = 0f;
                break;
            }
            if (t < cursor + typeMs + linePauseMs) {
                currentLine = i;
                visibleChars = line.length();
                liftFraction = (float)((t - cursor - typeMs) / (double)Math.max(1L, linePauseMs));
                break;
            }
            cursor += typeMs + linePauseMs;
            if (i == wrapped.size() - 1) {
                currentLine = i;
                visibleChars = line.length();
                liftFraction = 1f;
                finished = true;
            }
        }

        Graphics2D clip = (Graphics2D)g.create();
        clip.setClip(panelX + 28, panelY + 22, panelW - 56, panelH - 44);
        clip.setFont(crawlFont);
        int baseY = panelY + panelH - 44;
        int lift = Math.round(liftFraction * lineH);
        for (int i = Math.max(0, currentLine - 22); i <= currentLine && i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            String shown = line;
            if (i == currentLine && visibleChars < line.length()) shown = line.substring(0, Math.max(0, Math.min(visibleChars, line.length())));
            int yy = baseY - (currentLine - i) * lineH - lift;
            if (yy < panelY + 18 || yy > panelY + panelH - 8) continue;
            if (shown.isEmpty()) continue;
            int distanceFromCenter = Math.abs((panelY + panelH / 2) - yy);
            int alpha = Math.max(72, Math.min(238, 238 - distanceFromCenter / 3));
            clip.setColor(options.highContrastText ? Color.WHITE : new Color(224, 213, 166, alpha));
            center(clip, shown, panelX + panelW/2, yy);
        }
        // Subtle typewriter cursor on the actively printing line. It is centered
        // with the line so the crawl remains cinematic instead of becoming a
        // left-aligned terminal dump.
        if (currentLine < wrapped.size()) {
            String line = wrapped.get(currentLine);
            if (!line.isEmpty() && visibleChars < line.length() && ((elapsed / 360L) % 2L == 0L)) {
                String shown = line.substring(0, Math.max(0, Math.min(visibleChars, line.length())));
                int yy = baseY - lift;
                int sw = clip.getFontMetrics().stringWidth(shown);
                int cx = panelX + panelW / 2;
                int cursorX = cx - sw / 2 + sw + 4;
                if (yy >= panelY + 18 && yy <= panelY + panelH - 8) {
                    clip.setColor(new Color(224, 213, 166, 185));
                    clip.drawLine(cursorX, yy - fm.getAscent() + 2, cursorX, yy + 3);
                }
            }
        }
        clip.dispose();

        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.PLAIN, Math.max(10f, Math.min(12f, H / 62f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        center(g, "SKIP remains available in the lower right.", W/2, H-54);

        long textTotalMs = introCrawlTextDurationMillis(wrapped, leadInMs, charMs, blankMs, linePauseMs);
        long fullCrawlMs = Math.max(textTotalMs + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_TAIL_SAFETY_MS, INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_EXPECTED_MS + INTRO_CRAWL_AUDIO_TAIL_SAFETY_MS);
        if (elapsed > fullCrawlMs) continueFromIntroCrawl();
    }
```

```java
    void drawCharacter(Graphics2D g) {
        Candidate c = candidates.get(candidateIndex);
        JobProfile jp = JobProfile.get(c.jobs.get(jobIndex));
        boolean validJob = jp.meets(c);
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.BACKGROUND));
        g.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, 20, 20, W-40, H-40, "outer");
        g.setFont(titleFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(24f, Math.min(38f, H / 15f))));
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_TITLE)); center(g, "SELECT THE UNFORTUNATE", W/2, Math.max(54, H/10));

        int margin = Math.max(24, W / 34);
        int topY = Math.max(86, H / 7);
        int bh = Math.max(28, Math.min(38, H / 17));
        int gap = Math.max(8, W / 120);
        int nameY = topY + bh + 10;
        int colTop = nameY + 86;
        int colH = Math.max(210, H - colTop - 44);
        int availW = W - margin * 2 - gap * 2;
        int rangesW = Math.max(120, Math.min(160, availW / 5));
        int dossierW = Math.max(220, Math.min(310, availW / 3));
        int statsW = Math.max(260, availW - rangesW - dossierW - gap * 2);
        int rangesX = margin;
        int statsX = rangesX + rangesW + gap;
        int dossierX = statsX + statsW + gap;
        if (dossierX + dossierW > W - margin) {
            dossierW = Math.max(210, W - margin - dossierX);
            statsW = Math.max(250, dossierX - gap - statsX);
        }

        // Compact portrait + editable name band. The portrait is intentionally scaled so it no longer steals the central screen.
        int portraitSizeW = Math.max(62, Math.min(86, H / 6));
        int portraitX = margin + 10;
        int portraitY = nameY - 4;
        Graphics2D pg = (Graphics2D)g.create();
        double ps = portraitSizeW / 150.0;
        pg.translate(portraitX, portraitY);
        pg.scale(ps, ps);
        drawPortrait(pg, 0, 0, c);
        pg.dispose();
        int nameW = Math.min(460, Math.max(250, W - portraitX - portraitSizeW - margin - 32));
        characterNameEditRect.setBounds(Math.max(portraitX + portraitSizeW + 22, W - margin - nameW - 10), nameY + 2, nameW, 34);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(characterNameEditActive ? new Color(70, 58, 34) : new Color(28, 25, 22));
        g.fillRoundRect(characterNameEditRect.x, characterNameEditRect.y, characterNameEditRect.width, characterNameEditRect.height, 10, 10);
        g.setColor(characterNameEditActive ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        g.drawRoundRect(characterNameEditRect.x, characterNameEditRect.y, characterNameEditRect.width, characterNameEditRect.height, 10, 10);
        String nameLine = c.name + (characterNameEditActive && (frameCount / 18) % 2 == 0 ? "_" : "");
        FontMetrics nameFm = g.getFontMetrics();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(nameLine, nameFm, nameW - 20), characterNameEditRect.x + characterNameEditRect.width/2, nameY + 25);
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        int candX = portraitX + portraitSizeW + 8;
        int candY = portraitY + Math.max(20, portraitSizeW - 24);
        AgeAndWorldTimeAuthority.initializeCandidateAge(c, new Random(Objects.hash(c.name, c.portraitIndex, candidateIndex, seed)));
        String candLine = "Candidate " + (candidateIndex+1) + "/" + candidates.size() + " | " + c.ageYears + "y " + c.ageBand;
        g.setColor(new Color(18,17,15,220));
        int candW = Math.max(154, Math.min(220, characterNameEditRect.x - candX - 10));
        g.fillRoundRect(candX, candY, candW, 24, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(new Color(120,105,72));
        g.drawRoundRect(candX, candY, candW, 24, 8, 8);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        center(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(candLine, g.getFontMetrics(), candW - 10), candX + candW/2, candY + 17);

        // Left: thin roll range reference.
        drawPanelBox(g, rangesX, colTop, rangesW, colH, "ROLL RANGES");
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int ry = colTop + 50;
        for (String key : Candidate.statKeys()) {
            if (ry > colTop + colH - 70) break;
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(key + ": " + Candidate.statRangeText(key), g.getFontMetrics(), rangesW - 24), rangesX+12, ry);
            ry += 23;
        }
        g.setColor(new Color(190,140,110));
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap("Jobs may require base stats. Invalid work is marked red and blocked.", Math.max(16, (rangesW-24)/8))) {
            if (ry > colTop + colH - 16) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, line, rangesX+12, ry); ry += 16;
        }

        // Center: prioritized character sheet.
        g.setColor(new Color(20,20,20,225)); g.fillRect(statsX, colTop, statsW, colH);
        g.setColor(new Color(120,105,72)); g.drawRect(statsX, colTop, statsW, colH); stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "character-sheet-stats", statsX, colTop, statsW, colH);
        g.setFont(uiFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); drawUiTextLine(g, "CHARACTER SHEET", statsX+14, colTop+30);
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        int sx = statsX+16, sy = colTop+76;
        boolean twoCols = statsW >= 360;
        int colW = twoCols ? Math.max(190, statsW/2-8) : statsW - 28;
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_DIM));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "STAT", sx, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "BASE", sx+94, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "MOD", sx+134, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "TOTAL", sx+174, sy-20);
        if (twoCols) {
            int hx = sx + colW;
            drawUiTextLine(g, "STAT", hx, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "BASE", hx+94, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "MOD", hx+134, sy-20); drawUiTextLine(g, "TOTAL", hx+174, sy-20);
        }
        int row = 0;
        int rowsPerCol = twoCols ? 7 : Math.max(7, (colH - 96) / 22);
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : c.stats.entrySet()) {
            if (!twoCols && row >= rowsPerCol) break;
            int bonus = jp.statBonuses.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0) + jp.statPenalties.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0);
            int total = e.getValue() + bonus;
            int drawX = sx + (twoCols && row >= rowsPerCol ? colW : 0);
            int drawY = sy + (row % rowsPerCol) * 22;
            if (drawY > colTop + colH - 42) break;
            g.setColor(new Color(180,178,150));
            drawUiTextLine(g, e.getKey()+":", drawX, drawY);
            drawUiTextLine(g, String.format("%2d", e.getValue()), drawX+100, drawY);
            g.setColor(bonus < 0 ? new Color(185,70,60) : (bonus > 0 ? new Color(100,175,100) : new Color(145,142,120)));
            drawUiTextLine(g, bonus == 0 ? "--" : String.format("%+d", bonus), drawX+140, drawY);
            g.setColor(total < e.getValue() ? new Color(205,95,82) : (total > e.getValue() ? new Color(135,215,135) : new Color(190,188,158)));
            drawUiTextLine(g, String.format("%2d", total), drawX+184, drawY);
            row++;
        }
        g.setColor(validJob ? new Color(150,145,118) : new Color(235,95,75));
        int ledgerY = colTop + colH - 34;
        for (String line : TextSurfaceApi.wrap(validJob ? "Green modifiers help; red modifiers hurt. Final total after job." : "INVALID JOB: " + jp.missingText(c), Math.max(22, (statsW-34)/8))) {
            if (ledgerY > colTop + colH - 10) break;
            drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(line, g.getFontMetrics(), statsW-34), statsX+18, ledgerY);
            ledgerY += Math.max(14, g.getFontMetrics().getHeight());
        }

        // Right: lower-priority dossier, scrollable inside its own panel.
        g.setColor(new Color(22,21,19,232)); g.fillRect(dossierX, colTop, dossierW, colH);
        g.setColor(validJob ? new Color(145,122,78) : new Color(180,55,45)); g.drawRect(dossierX, colTop, dossierW, colH);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT)); drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel(jobDossierTab==0 ? "JOB DOSSIER: " + jp.name : "MASTER JOB LIST", g.getFontMetrics(), dossierW-28), dossierX+14, colTop+66);
        if (!validJob) {
            g.setFont(uiFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(20f, uiFont.getSize2D()+6f)));
            g.setColor(new Color(245,95,80));
            center(g, "INVALID JOB", dossierX + dossierW/2, colTop + 92);
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        ArrayList<String> dossier = new ArrayList<>();
        if (jobDossierTab == 1) {
            dossier.add("JOB | STATUS | FACTION | CLOTHING | REQUIREMENTS");
            dossier.add("Use < JOB / JOB > to select an entry; the table remains separated from the dossier text.");
            dossier.add("");
            for (int i=0; i<c.jobs.size(); i++) {
                JobProfile p = JobProfile.get(c.jobs.get(i));
                boolean ok = p.meets(c);
                dossier.add((i==jobIndex?"> ":"  ") + p.name + " | " + (ok ? "VALID" : "INVALID: " + p.missingText(c)) + " | " + p.faction.label + " | " + p.clothingName);
                dossier.add("    Req: " + p.requirementText());
                dossier.add("");
            }
        } else {
            dossier.addAll(TextSurfaceApi.wrap(jp.description, Math.max(24, (dossierW-42)/8)));
            dossier.add("");
            dossier.add("Requirements: " + jp.requirementText());
            dossier.add(validJob ? "Requirement check: PASSED" : "Requirement check: FAILED — " + jp.missingText(c));
            dossier.add("Bonuses: " + jp.bonusText());
            dossier.add("Penalties: " + jp.penaltyText());
            dossier.add("Faction affiliation: " + jp.faction.label);
            dossier.add("Starting clothes: " + jp.clothingName + " | Defense " + jp.clothingDefense + " | Disguise cover " + jp.disguiseBase + "%");
            dossier.add("");
            dossier.add("Starting inventory:");
            for (String item : jp.startingItems()) dossier.add("- " + item);
            dossier.add("");
            if (jp.faction == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS) dossier.add("Warning: most gangers will treat this start as a walking arrest warrant.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.BANDIT) dossier.add("Warning: law enforcement and rival crews will not admire your career path.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.SCAVENGER) dossier.add("Scavenger-aligned clothing is broadly tolerated, except by bandits, and often questioned by Civic Wardens patrols.");
            else if (jp.faction == Faction.NONE) dossier.add("No faction backing. Better skills, fewer friends, and the full warmth of underhive hospitality.");
            else dossier.add("Faction-aligned start. Your clothes open some doors and paint a target on your back for enemy factions.");
            if (jp.faction != Faction.NONE) dossier.add("Affiliation rule: true members of this faction do not roll disguise checks against their own faction merely because of clothing.");
        }
        drawScrollableWrappedLines(g, dossier, dossierX+14, colTop+96, dossierW-36, colH-126, jobDossierScroll, jobDossierTab==0?"job-dossier":"job-list");
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        drawUiTextLine(g, GuiLayoutApi.fitLabel("Scroll with wheel/drag/arrows/PgUp/PgDn", g.getFontMetrics(), dossierW-28), dossierX+14, colTop+colH-12);
        g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(new Color(150,145,118));
        center(g, "Top row changes candidate/job; center sheet is primary; dossier and roll ranges remain bounded and scrollable.", W/2, H-24);
    }
```

```java
    java.util.List<String> roomInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (entry.endsWith(" Rooms")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.length() - " Rooms".length());
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Zone room set");
            lines.add("Scope: describes the room pool for " + zoneName + ", not the whole zone and not a specific room instance.");
            lines.add("Layout rule: rooms are enclosed first, doors are placed on valid room walls, and corridors attach outward from door points.");
            lines.add("Room bias: " + (z==null?"generic underhive rooms":zoneGenerationRole(z)));
            lines.add("Inspectable texture: " + (z==null?InspectableFeatureTable.sampleLine():InspectableFeatureTable.combinedFor(z, new Random(31), "sample").replace("sample; inspectable features: ", "")) + ".");
            lines.add("Special hooks: traders, locked caches, faction access, machinery, shrines, vending machines, or encounter logic are selected from this zone's room pool.");
        } else if (entry.contains(" Generic: ")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.indexOf(" Generic: ")).trim();
            String name = entry.substring(entry.indexOf(" Generic: ") + " Generic: ".length()).trim();
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Generic room sample");
            lines.add("Zone context: " + zoneName + " — " + (z==null?"generic room pool":zoneGenerationRole(z)) + ".");
            lines.add("Sample name: " + name + ".");
            lines.add("Generation rule: common rooms use this zone's size bias, faction bias, loot list, content symbols, and inspectable feature table.");
            lines.add("Purpose: fills " + zoneName + " with believable functional clutter while keeping special rooms rarer and more meaningful.");
        } else if (entry.contains(" Special: ")) {
            String zoneName = entry.substring(0, entry.indexOf(" Special: ")).trim();
            String name = entry.substring(entry.indexOf(" Special: ") + " Special: ".length()).trim();
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(zoneName);
            lines.add("Special room sample");
            lines.add("Zone context: " + zoneName + " — " + (z==null?"generic special-room pool":zoneGenerationRole(z)) + ".");
            lines.add("Sample name: " + name + ".");
            lines.add("Generation rule: special rooms are inserted after ordinary room selection and can override contents with themed fixtures or actors.");
            lines.add("Player use: inspect before interacting; " + zoneName + " specials are where services, story hooks, danger, and operational surfaces appear.");
        } else {
            lines.add("Room reference");
            lines.add("This entry identifies a generated room concept. The current generator gives each room walls, doors, floor area, inspectable texture, and a zone/faction context.");
        }
        return lines;
    }
```

```java
    java.util.List<String> combatInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Combat Command":
                lines.add("Attack command reference");
                lines.add("Use the COMBAT button or F hotkey to attack an adjacent hostile using carried/equipped weapon logic or bare hands.");
                lines.add("Each attack spends action time and reports hit, miss, armor soak, wounds, and incapacitation through RECENT ACTIONS.");
                break;
            case "Hit Chance and Defense":
                lines.add("Accuracy and defense reference");
                lines.add("Hit chance compares attack skill, weapon suitability, target defense/agility, and situational cover logic.");
                lines.add("Failed attacks still produce explicit feedback so the player knows whether the problem was range, target state, weapon, or chance.");
                break;
            case "Damage and Armor":
                lines.add("Damage resolution reference");
                lines.add("Weapon or base attack damage is reduced by armor before body damage is applied to a rolled location.");
                lines.add("Armor therefore changes expected injury, not just whether an enemy is allowed to exist after being clicked.");
                break;
            case "Targeted Attacks":
                lines.add("Targeting system reference");
                lines.add("Reserved targeting should trade hit chance for tactical reward: disarming arms, slowing legs, stunning heads, or damaging torso stability.");
                lines.add("This entry is intentionally distinct from default attacks, which currently roll a random body location for speed and danger.");
                break;
            case "Body Injuries and Incapacitation":
                lines.add("Combat injury reference");
                lines.add("Damaged legs slow movement, damaged arms and hands penalize weapon/tool use, and severe body or head damage risks incapacitation.");
                lines.add("Current body pressure: crippled legs " + crippledLegCount() + ", crippled arms/hands " + crippledArmCount() + ", wounds " + wounds + ".");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("Hostile intent bark reference");
                lines.add("Enemies that see or hear the player can announce intent in the action feed before or as combat begins.");
                lines.add("Purpose: make danger readable without granting perfect tactical information through the map display.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:3220-3251
Kind: method
Name: drawInfopediaEntryList
SHA256: 5e5e88454d2fa2f6e24ba237e0661e1f19a2dac3c5c6d6568533ad67c191115b

```java
    void drawInfopediaEntryList(Graphics2D g, java.util.List<String> entries, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(20, fm.getHeight()+4);
        int visible = Math.max(1, h / lineH);
        int maxScroll = Math.max(0, entries.size() - visible);
        infopediaScroll = Math.max(0, Math.min(infopediaScroll, maxScroll));
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(x-4,y-4,w+8,h+8);
        int yy = y + lineH;
        for(int row=0; row<visible; row++) {
            int idx = infopediaScroll + row;
            if (idx >= entries.size()) break;
            boolean sel = idx == infopediaSelected;
            if (sel) {
                g.setColor(new Color(80,65,30,220));
                g.fillRoundRect(x-6, yy-lineH+3, w+4, lineH, 8, 8);
            }
            g.setColor(sel ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            String label = (sel ? "> " : "  ") + entries.get(idx);
            g.drawString(label, x, yy);
            yy += lineH;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
        int sbX=x+w+10, sbY=y, sbW=14, sbH=h;
        g.setColor(new Color(20,18,14,235)); g.fillRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        g.setColor(new Color(108,92,58)); g.drawRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        int th=maxScroll<=0?h:Math.max(28,h*visible/Math.max(visible,entries.size())); int ty=maxScroll<=0?y:y+(h-th)*infopediaScroll/maxScroll;
        g.setColor("infopedia-list".equals(activeScrollTag)?optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT):new Color(220,190,105));
        g.fillRect(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3));
        scrollRegions.add(new ScrollRegion("infopedia-list", new Rectangle(sbX, sbY, sbW, sbH), new Rectangle(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3)), maxScroll, visible, infopediaScroll));
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:3341-3391

Name: clampButtonsToVisibleMenuBounds
SHA256: 8efb6346ef0d0a64bd51f6cafb8005c4acf00701af107bded8abf2b441693955

```java
    void clampButtonsToVisibleMenuBounds() {
        int W = getWidth(), H = getHeight();
        Rectangle screenSafe = new Rectangle(12, 12, Math.max(1, W - 24), Math.max(1, H - 24));
        Rectangle optionPanelSafe = optionPanelInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle commandSafe = commandPanelInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle inventoryActionSafe = inventoryActionInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle worldSetupActionSafe = worldSetupActionInnerSafeRect();
        Rectangle saveLoadSafe = saveLoadButtonSafeRect();

        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            Rectangle safe = screenSafe;
            if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = isGraphicsDropdownButton(b) ? graphicsDropdownInnerRect() : optionPanelSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD") ? worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect() : worldSetupActionSafe;
            else if (isCommandSurfaceButton(b)) safe = commandSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY && isInventoryActionButton(b)) safe = inventoryActionSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = saveLoadSafe;
            fitButtonInto(b, safe);
        }

        if (screen == Screen.GAME) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = commandSurfaceButtons();
            flowButtonGroup(group, commandSafe, 1);
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = inventoryActionButtons();
            flowButtonGroup(group, inventoryActionSafe, 1);
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD) {
            flowSaveLoadButtons();
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelUsesCommandSurface()) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> group = commandSurfaceButtons();
            int cols = group.size() > 14 || panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH ? 2 : 1;
            flowButtonGroup(group, commandSafe, cols);
        } else if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS) {
            flowOptionsButtons(optionPanelSafe);
        } else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP) {
            java.util.List<ButtonBox> actionGroup = new ArrayList<>();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK") && !b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD")) actionGroup.add(b);
            flowButtonGroup(actionGroup, worldSetupActionSafe, 2);
            Rectangle genSafe = worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) if (b.label != null && b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD")) { b.r = new Rectangle(genSafe.x, genSafe.y, genSafe.width, Math.max(22, Math.min(30, genSafe.height))); }
        }

        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            Rectangle safe = screenSafe;
            if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = isGraphicsDropdownButton(b) ? graphicsDropdownInnerRect() : optionPanelSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.WORLD_SETUP && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = b.label.equals("GENERATE WORLD") ? worldSetupGenerateInnerSafeRect() : worldSetupActionSafe;
            else if (isCommandSurfaceButton(b)) safe = commandSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INVENTORY && isInventoryActionButton(b)) safe = inventoryActionSafe;
            else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD && b.label != null && !b.label.equals("BACK")) safe = saveLoadSafe;
            fitButtonInto(b, safe);
        }
    }
```

Name: applySemanticButtonIcons
SHA256: 9762f5e844e876961e83828b1bc45c66b2e72bc5ea5a35b5faed4cc613ec9f6c

```java
    void applySemanticButtonIcons() {
        if (buttons == null || buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        if (screen == Screen.PANEL && (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH)) {
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
                if (b == null || b.label == null || "BACK".equals(b.label)) continue;
                if (b.label.startsWith("DEF INFO") || b.label.startsWith("VALIDATE") || b.label.startsWith("CLAIM") || b.label.startsWith("STASH") || b.label.startsWith("TAKE") || b.label.startsWith("DRINK") || b.label.startsWith("SECURITY")) continue;
                BufferedImage icon = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForName(b.label));
                if (icon != null) b.icon = icon;
                if (b.tip != null && !b.tip.contains("Semantic object asset:")) b.tip = b.tip + " " + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.semanticSummaryForName(b.label);
            }
        } else if (screen == Screen.EDITOR) {
            String category = inGameEditorPaletteCategory();
            for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
                if (b == null || b.label == null) continue;
                String clean = b.label.replace("▶", "").trim();
                if (clean.isBlank() || clean.equals("BACK") || clean.startsWith("NEW") || clean.equals("UNDO") || clean.equals("REDO") || clean.startsWith("HELP")) continue;
                String id = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForEditorPalette(category, clean);
                BufferedImage icon = ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.imageForAssetId(id);
                if (icon != null) b.icon = icon;
                if (b.tip != null && !b.tip.contains("assetId=")) b.tip = b.tip + " assetId=" + id + ".";
            }
        }
    }
```

```java
    void stampUiFrameId(Graphics2D g, String prefix, String label, int x, int y, int w, int h) {
        if (g == null || w < 28 || h < 18) return;
        String safePrefix = prefix == null ? "F" : prefix;
        int hash = Math.abs(Objects.hash(safePrefix, label, x/3, y/3, w/3, h/3, screen, panelMode)) % 10000;
        String id = safePrefix + String.format(Locale.US, "%04d", hash);
        Font oldFont = g.getFont();
        Color oldColor = g.getColor();
        g.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, 9));
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int tw = fm.stringWidth(id);
        int bx = Math.max(x + 2, x + w - tw - 6);
        int by = y + 3;
        g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,188));
        g.fillRect(bx - 2, by, tw + 4, fm.getHeight() + 1);
        g.setColor(new Color(245,220,130));
        g.drawString(id, bx, by + fm.getAscent());
        g.setFont(oldFont);
        g.setColor(oldColor);
    }
```

```java
    Rectangle graphicsDropdownOuterRect() {
        if (screen != Screen.OPTIONS || graphicsDropdown < 0 || (optionsTab != 0 && optionsTab != 1 && optionsTab != 4)) return new Rectangle(0,0,0,0);
        int w = getWidth(), h = getHeight();
        Rectangle optionSafe = optionControlInnerSafeRect();
        int requestedCols = optionsTab == 7 ? 4 : 3;
        int colGap = Math.max(6, GuiLayoutApi.columnGap(uiScaleFactor()) - 4);
        int bw = Math.max(104, (optionSafe.width - colGap * (requestedCols - 1)) / requestedCols);
        int gap = bw + colGap;
        int y = optionSafe.y;
        int itemCount;
        int x;
        int ddY;
        int ddW;
        if (graphicsDropdown == 0) {
            itemCount = 3; x = optionSafe.x; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 1) {
            itemCount = Math.min(DisplayResolutionAuthority.choiceCount(), Math.max(8, Math.min(14, optionSafe.height / Math.max(22, scaled(26))))); x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = y + Math.max(24, Math.min(34, optionSafe.height / 6)); ddW = bw * 2 + colGap;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 2) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.PALETTE_NAMES.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = optionsTab == 4 ? y + scaled(198) : y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 3) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.DOWNSCALE_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 4) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.TARGET_FPS_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 5) {
            itemCount = GameOptions.RENDER_QUALITY_LABELS.length; x = optionSafe.x + gap*2; ddY = y + scaled(42); ddW = bw;
        } else return new Rectangle(0,0,0,0);
        int rowH = Math.max(26, scaled(30));
        int ddH = Math.max(rowH + 18, 18 + itemCount * rowH + Math.max(0, itemCount - 1) * scaled(4));
        Rectangle controls = optionControlInnerSafeRect();
        int maxBottom = Math.max(controls.y + controls.height + 24, getHeight() - 76);
        if (ddY + ddH > maxBottom) ddY = Math.max(controls.y, maxBottom - ddH);
        int minX = Math.max(24, optionPanelInnerSafeRect().x);
        int maxX = Math.max(minX, optionPanelInnerSafeRect().x + optionPanelInnerSafeRect().width - ddW);
        x = Math.max(minX, Math.min(x, maxX));
        return new Rectangle(x, ddY, Math.max(120, ddW), ddH);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:3570-3578
Kind: method
Name: isCommandSurfaceButton
SHA256: 497a340ef3939c687f268a9df9bc46c68265dffad54e01011a3dd19155b11aca

```java
    boolean isCommandSurfaceButton(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null || b.label == null || b.label.equals("BACK")) return false;
        // Phase 4 containment rule: command-surface membership is semantic, not
        // geometric. Several older panels originally placed their buttons beside or
        // below the command tablet and then expected later code to corral them. If
        // we decide membership by rectangle intersection, those off-frame buttons
        // are never reclaimed and can spill down the screen.
        return screen == Screen.GAME || (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelUsesCommandSurface());
    }
```

```java
    void activateSelectedButtonUniversal() {
        if (buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        selectedButton = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedButton, buttons.size()-1));
        ButtonBox b = buttons.get(selectedButton);
        if (!buttonIsModalInteractive(b)) { sounds.play("panelClose", options); return; }
        sounds.play("button", options);
        DebugLog.audit("UI_BUTTON_CONFIRM", "label=" + b.label + " via E/Enter | " + stateSummary());
        runGuarded("BUTTON", "universal confirm " + b.label, b.action);
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void drawPortrait(Graphics2D g, int x, int y, Candidate c) {
        g.setColor(new Color(22,22,24)); g.fillRect(x,y,140,150);
        g.setColor(new Color(160,150,110)); g.drawRect(x,y,140,150);
        NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry locked = NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.unlockedEntry(cachedOperatorProfileName, c == null ? "" : c.name);
        BufferedImage face = null;
        String portraitLabel = "IMPORTED DOSSIER";
        if (locked != null) {
            face = images.getNameLockedProfilePortrait(locked.key);
            portraitLabel = "PROFILE DOSSIER";
            if (c != null) c.nameLockedProfileKey = locked.key;
        }
        if (face == null && c != null) face = images.getPortrait(c.portraitSheet, c.portraitIndex);
        if (face != null) {
            g.drawImage(face, x+6, y+6, 128, 128, null);
            g.setFont(smallFont); g.setColor(new Color(190,180,130));
            g.drawString(portraitLabel, x+10, y+145);
        } else {
            g.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, 18));
            for (int i=0;i<c.portrait.length;i++) g.drawString(c.portrait[i], x+30, y+35+i*20);
        }
    }
```

Name: virtualUiLayout
SHA256: 14aa1019ee20fc55fc16977ab7e4b582a53c28ff9f1f2015586f9c22dc74da93

```java
    UiLayout virtualUiLayout() {
        // Input events are mapped from physical Swing pixels into the fixed virtual
        // render canvas before they reach gameplay code. Mouse-to-tile conversion
        // must therefore use the same virtual layout that drawGame used, not the
        // live Swing panel bounds; otherwise zoom/letterbox scaling pulls targeting
        // toward the upper-left corner.
        if (screen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT) return UiLayout.computeSectorAudit(renderScaling.virtualWidth(), renderScaling.virtualHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
        return UiLayout.compute(renderScaling.virtualWidth(), renderScaling.virtualHeight(), uiScaleFactor());
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:4116-4132
Kind: method
Name: drawTrapWarningOverlays
SHA256: 29f542620cb21910722550a0c959899e955b7932e28d90edd63452d5197750cb

```java
    void drawTrapWarningOverlays(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || world.trapRecords == null || world.trapRecords.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(9, Math.min(14, cellH/2))));
        for (TrapRecord t : world.trapRecords) {
            if (t == null || t.x < camX || t.y < camY || t.x >= camX + cols || t.y >= camY + rows) continue;
            boolean visibleTrap = !t.hidden || "revealed".equals(t.state) || "triggered".equals(t.state) || "disarmed".equals(t.state);
            if (!visibleTrap && !(isVisible(t.x,t.y) && stat("Intellect",5)*5 >= t.detectionDifficulty)) continue;
            int px = ox + (t.x - camX) * cellW, yy = (tileIconMode()? oy + (t.y-camY)*cellH : oy + (t.y-camY)*cellH - cellH + 3);
            float alpha = "triggered".equals(t.state) ? 0.35f : ("disarmed".equals(t.state) ? 0.25f : 0.70f);
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
            gg.setColor(new Color(245, 165, 35));
            gg.drawRect(px+3, yy+3, Math.max(2,cellW-7), Math.max(2,cellH-7));
            gg.drawString("T", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), yy + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:4140-4180
Kind: method
Name: drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays
SHA256: f647d3c4f313cbdd2ce7abe1193d567c943174d34c7b2ba8d7689d7e41deba2b

```java
    void drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || world.hazardWarnings == null || world.hazardWarnings.isEmpty()) return;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        int tri = Math.max(8, Math.min(16, Math.min(cellW, cellH) / 2));
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(9, Math.min(15, tri))));
        for (EnvironmentalHazardRecord h : world.hazardWarnings) {
            if (h == null || h.x < camX || h.y < camY || h.x >= camX + cols || h.y >= camY + rows) continue;
            boolean vis = isVisible(h.x, h.y), rem = isRemembered(h.x, h.y);
            if (!vis && !rem) continue;
            int px = ox + (h.x - camX) * cellW, py = oy + (h.y - camY) * cellH;
            float alpha = vis ? 0.82f : 0.34f;
            int frame = Math.floorMod(turn + h.phase, 3);
            int yy = tileIconMode() ? py : py - cellH + 3;
            Color c = h.color();
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, Math.min(0.42f, alpha * (0.24f + 0.08f * frame))));
            gg.setColor(c);
            if (h.family.contains("wire") || h.family.contains("electric")) {
                int y0 = yy + Math.max(3, cellH/3);
                gg.drawLine(px + 2, y0, px + cellW/3, yy + cellH - 3);
                gg.drawLine(px + cellW/3, yy + cellH - 3, px + (cellW*2)/3, yy + 4);
                gg.drawLine(px + (cellW*2)/3, yy + 4, px + cellW - 3, yy + Math.max(4, cellH/2));
            } else if (h.family.contains("sludge") || h.family.contains("runoff")) {
                gg.fillOval(px + Math.max(1, frame), yy + cellH/3, Math.max(6, cellW - 4), Math.max(4, cellH/3));
                gg.drawArc(px + 2, yy + 2, Math.max(6, cellW - 5), Math.max(6, cellH - 5), frame * 40, 180);
            } else {
                gg.drawArc(px + 2 + frame, yy + 3, Math.max(6, cellW - 5), Math.max(6, cellH/2), 20, 220);
                gg.drawArc(px + 4, yy + Math.max(4, cellH/3), Math.max(5, cellW - 8), Math.max(6, cellH/2), 210, 220);
                gg.drawString("~", px + Math.max(2, cellW/3), yy + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
            }
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
            gg.setColor(new Color(220, 35, 28));
            gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(1.0f, Math.min(2.0f, cellW / 18.0f))));
            gg.drawRect(px + 1, yy + 1, Math.max(1, cellW - 3), Math.max(1, cellH - 3));
            int[] xs = {px + cellW - tri - 1, px + cellW - 1, px + cellW - tri/2 - 1};
            int[] ys = {yy + 1, yy + 1, yy + tri + 1};
            gg.fillPolygon(xs, ys, 3);
            gg.setColor(Color.BLACK);
            gg.drawString("!", px + cellW - tri + Math.max(1, tri/4), yy + Math.max(10, tri));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:4246-4279

Name: drawCombatAnimations
SHA256: 2452751eed6e5f45ce9c846279fa1dfca991f8ad0f2217d7c7c85e263bb82997

```java
    void drawCombatAnimations(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (combatAnimations.isEmpty()) return;
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(18, cellH/2))));
        for (CombatAnimation a : combatAnimations) {
            double t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, (now - a.startMillis) / (double)Math.max(1, a.durationMillis)));
            int frame = (int)Math.floor(t * 8.0);
            if (weaponIsMeleeAnimation(a.weapon)) {
                int sx = a.x0 - camX, sy = a.y0 - camY;
                if (sx >= 0 && sy >= 0 && sx < cols && sy < rows) {
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, (float)(0.9 - t * 0.45)));
                    gg.setColor(a.hit ? new Color(245, 230, 190) : new Color(210, 160, 120));
                    gg.drawString(projectileGlyphForWeapon(a.weapon, a.hit, frame), ox + sx*cellW + Math.max(2, cellW/4), oy + sy*cellH + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
                }
                continue;
            }
            ArrayList<Point> pts = linePoints(a.x0, a.y0, a.x1, a.y1);
            int max = Math.max(1, pts.size()-1);
            int idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(max, (int)Math.round(t * max)));
            for (int j=Math.max(0, idx-2); j<=Math.min(max, idx+1); j++) {
                Point p = pts.get(j);
                int sx = p.x - camX, sy = p.y - camY;
                if (sx < 0 || sy < 0 || sx >= cols || sy >= rows) continue;
                float alpha = (float)Math.max(0.12, 0.88 - Math.abs(idx-j)*0.22 - t*0.25);
                gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, alpha));
                String glyph = projectileGlyphForWeapon(a.weapon, a.hit, frame + j);
                if (!a.hit && j == idx && (frame % 2 == 0)) glyph = glyph.replace('~', '.');
                gg.setColor(a.hit ? new Color(255, 205, 145) : new Color(240, 120, 80));
                gg.drawString(glyph, ox + sx*cellW + Math.max(1, cellW/8), oy + sy*cellH + Math.max(12, (cellH*2)/3));
            }
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

```java
    void drawExplosionAnimations(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (explosionAnimations.isEmpty()) return;
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(20, cellH/2))));
        for (ExplosionAnimation a : explosionAnimations) {
            double t = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, (now - a.startMillis) / (double)Math.max(1, a.durationMillis)));
            if (a.grenadeArc) {
                int x = (int)Math.round(a.x0 + (a.x1 - a.x0) * t);
                int y = (int)Math.round(a.y0 + (a.y1 - a.y0) * t);
                if (x >= camX && y >= camY && x < camX+cols && y < camY+rows) {
                    int px=ox+(x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(y-camY)*cellH;
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.85f));
                    gg.setColor((System.currentTimeMillis()/120)%2==0 ? new Color(255,30,30) : new Color(255,190,70));
                    gg.drawString("*", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
                }
            } else {
                int ring = Math.max(0, Math.min(a.radius, (int)Math.ceil(t * (a.radius+1))));
                for (int x=a.x1-ring; x<=a.x1+ring; x++) for (int y=a.y1-ring; y<=a.y1+ring; y++) {
                    int d = Math.max(Math.abs(x-a.x1), Math.abs(y-a.y1));
                    if (d != ring || x < camX || y < camY || x >= camX+cols || y >= camY+rows) continue;
                    int px=ox+(x-camX)*cellW, py=oy+(y-camY)*cellH;
                    gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, (float)Math.max(0.15, 0.9 - t*0.55)));
                    gg.setColor(new Color(255, 115, 40));
                    gg.drawString("O", px + Math.max(3,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3));
                }
            }
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

```java
    void drawCombatTargetOverlay(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || !(screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT) || !combatCursorActive) return;
        if (combatX < 0 || combatY < 0 || combatX >= world.w || combatY >= world.h) return;
        TargetingSolution ts = targetingSolutionAt(combatX, combatY);
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        Stroke old = gg.getStroke();
        gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(Math.max(1.0f, cellW/12.0f), BasicStroke.CAP_BUTT, BasicStroke.JOIN_BEVEL, 1.0f, new float[]{7.0f, 5.0f}, 0.0f));

        gg.setColor(new Color(185, 25, 30));
        int px = ox + (playerX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
        int py = oy + (playerY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
        int tx = ox + (combatX - camX) * cellW + cellW/2;
        int ty = oy + (combatY - camY) * cellH + cellH/2;
        gg.drawLine(px, py, tx, ty);
        gg.setStroke(old);
        if (combatX >= camX && combatY >= camY && combatX < camX + cols && combatY < camY + rows) {
            int sx = combatX - camX, sy = combatY - camY;
            int rx = ox + sx * cellW, ry = oy + sy * cellH;

            gg.drawRect(rx - 2, ry - 2, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry - 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + Math.max(2, cellH/4));
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH + 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH - Math.max(2, cellH/4));
            gg.drawLine(rx - 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            gg.drawLine(rx + cellW + 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + cellW - Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            gg.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, Math.min(16, cellH/2))));
            gg.setColor(ts.hitPercent <= 0 ? new Color(230,90,80) : new Color(255,210,170));
            gg.drawString(ts.hitPercent + "%", rx + Math.max(1, cellW/5), ry - 4);
        }
        gg.dispose();
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:4370-4402

Name: beginManualMovementPlan
SHA256: 4eb5a5ea7aad35ec475078ed2751d513850652083f3503cf872ab5f1531824a4

```java
    void beginManualMovementPlan() {
        if (world == null || screen != Screen.GAME) return;
        manualMovementPlanActive = true;
        Point approach = selectedInteractionApproachTile();
        if (approach != null) {
            updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(approach.x, approach.y);
            manualMovementPlanActive = true;
            logEvent("Movement target planning: approaching " + interactionTargetLabel(lookX, lookY) + " from " + approach.x + "," + approach.y + ". Confirm with Enter/E/Space, cancel with Escape.");
            repaint();
            return;
        }
        int tx = playerX;
        int ty = playerY;
        int dx = lastMoveDx == 0 && lastMoveDy == 0 ? 1 : lastMoveDx;
        int dy = lastMoveDx == 0 && lastMoveDy == 0 ? 0 : lastMoveDy;
        for (int i = 0; i < Math.max(1, movementModeRange()); i++) {
            int nx = playerX + dx * (i + 1);
            int ny = playerY + dy * (i + 1);
            if (world.inBounds(nx, ny) && world.walkable(nx, ny)) { tx = nx; ty = ny; }
            else break;
        }
        if (tx == playerX && ty == playerY) {
            int[][] dirs = {{1,0},{0,1},{-1,0},{0,-1}};
            for (int[] d : dirs) {
                int nx = playerX + d[0], ny = playerY + d[1];
                if (world.inBounds(nx, ny) && world.walkable(nx, ny)) { tx = nx; ty = ny; break; }
            }
        }
        updateMouseMovementPreviewTo(tx, ty);
        manualMovementPlanActive = true;
        logEvent("Movement target planning: nudge with arrows or WASD, confirm with Enter/E/Space, cancel with Escape.");
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void drawMovementGhostPath(Graphics2D g, int camX, int camY, int cols, int rows, int ox, int oy, int cellW, int cellH) {
        if (world == null || screen != Screen.GAME || buildPlacementActive || movementModeRange() <= 1 || !movementGhostArmed) return;
        updateMoveGhostTarget(armedMoveDx == 0 && armedMoveDy == 0 ? lastMoveDx : armedMoveDx, armedMoveDy == 0 && armedMoveDx == 0 ? lastMoveDy : armedMoveDy);
        if (moveGhostX < 0 || moveGhostY < 0 || (moveGhostX == playerX && moveGhostY == playerY)) return;
        int dx = Integer.compare(moveGhostX, playerX);
        int dy = Integer.compare(moveGhostY, playerY);
        if (Math.abs(moveGhostX - playerX) > 0) dy = 0;
        else dx = 0;
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.33f));
        gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255));
        int tx = playerX, ty = playerY;
        for (int i=0; i<movementModeRange(); i++) {
            tx += dx; ty += dy;
            if (tx < 0 || ty < 0 || world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty) || !world.walkable(tx, ty)) break;
            if (tx >= camX && ty >= camY && tx < camX + cols && ty < camY + rows) {
                int px = ox + (tx - camX) * cellW;
                int py = oy + (ty - camY) * cellH;
                gg.drawRect(px + Math.max(1, cellW/5), py + Math.max(1, cellH/5), Math.max(3, (cellW*3)/5), Math.max(3, (cellH*3)/5));
            }
            if (tx == moveGhostX && ty == moveGhostY) break;
        }
        if (moveGhostX >= camX && moveGhostY >= camY && moveGhostX < camX + cols && moveGhostY < camY + rows) {
            int px = ox + (moveGhostX - camX) * cellW;
            int py = oy + (moveGhostY - camY) * cellH;
            BufferedImage face = activePortraitImage();
            gg.setComposite(AlphaComposite.getInstance(AlphaComposite.SRC_OVER, 0.42f));
            if (tileIconMode() && face != null) drawCachedMapImage(gg, face, px, py, cellW, cellH);
            else { gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255)); gg.drawString("@", px + Math.max(2,cellW/3), py + Math.max(12,(cellH*2)/3)); }
            gg.setColor(new Color(180, 220, 255));
            gg.drawRect(px+1, py+1, Math.max(3, cellW-3), Math.max(3, cellH-3));
        }
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

```java
    void drawRecentActionFeed(Graphics2D g) {

        Rectangle tactical = tacticalSlateRect();
        int x = tactical.x;
        int w = tactical.width;
        int y;
        int h;

            h = Math.max(64, Math.min(90, tactical.y - (map.y + map.height) - 6));
            y = Math.max(map.y + map.height + 2, tactical.y - h - 4);
            if (y + h > tactical.y - 2) h = Math.max(48, tactical.y - y - 3);

            y = tactical.y;
            h = tactical.height;

        Font labelFont = smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-4f));
        g.setFont(labelFont);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
        g.drawString(tacticalSlateVisible ? "RECENT ACTIONS" : "RECENT EVENTS — EXTERNAL AWARENESS", x + 12, y + 16);
        int bodyX = x + 12, bodyY = y + 22, bodyW = w - 24, bodyH = Math.max(14, h - 28);
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(bodyX, bodyY, bodyW, bodyH);
        g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-3f)));
        fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(12, fm.getHeight());
        int maxLines = Math.max(1, bodyH / lineH);
        ArrayList<String> source = new ArrayList<>();
        for (int i = Math.max(0, eventLog.size() - 80); i < eventLog.size(); i++) {
            String line = eventLog.get(i);
            if (recentFeedExternalAwarenessEligible(line)) source.add(line);
        }
        if (source.isEmpty()) source.add("No external events in immediate awareness.");
        java.util.List<String> wrapped = TextLayoutAuthority.wrapAllPixels(g, g.getFont(), source, bodyW - 8);
        int start = Math.max(0, wrapped.size() - maxLines);
        int yy = bodyY + fm.getAscent();
        for (int i = start; i < wrapped.size(); i++) {
            String line = wrapped.get(i);
            g.setColor(actionFeedColor(line));
            g.drawString(line, bodyX, yy);
            yy += lineH;
            if (yy > bodyY + bodyH) break;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
    }
```

```java
        slate.add(nameLine + " | Survival " + timeText() + " | World " + worldTimeText() + " | Food " + food + "/15 Water " + water + "/15 | Sleep " + (sleepNeed / TURNS_PER_HOUR) + "h/26h | Heat " + gangHeat + " Suspicion " + suspicion + " | XP " + xp + " KC " + knowledgeCredits + " | Camera " + camX + "," + camY + " | Zoom " + options.worldZoomLabel());
        slate.add("Move " + movementModeLabel() + " range " + movementModeRange() + " cost " + movementTurnCost() + " | " + activeMotionStateLabel() + " facing " + facingLabel() + " | vision " + visionRange() + " hearing " + hearingRange());
        slate.add(portableLightStatusLine());
        WorldSnapshot serverSnapshot = singlePlayerSectorBridge == null ? null : singlePlayerSectorBridge.latestWorldSnapshot();
        String serverAction = serverSnapshot == null || serverSnapshot.player() == null ? (singlePlayerSectorBridge == null ? "" : singlePlayerSectorBridge.activeActionDisplayLine()) : serverSnapshot.player().activeAction();
        if (serverAction != null && !serverAction.isBlank() && !"none".equalsIgnoreCase(serverAction)) slate.add("Server action: " + serverAction);
        if (serverSnapshot != null) slate.add("Server snapshot v" + serverSnapshot.version() + " | tiles " + serverSnapshot.visibleTiles().size() + " | NPCs " + serverSnapshot.visibleNpcs().size() + " | objects " + serverSnapshot.visibleObjects().size());
        slate.add(tacticalPromptLine());
        int yy = r.y + 32;
        java.util.List<String> wrappedSlate = TextLayoutAuthority.wrapAllPixels(g, g.getFont(), slate, r.width - 36);
        for (String wrapped : wrappedSlate) {
            if (yy > r.y + r.height - 10) { g.setClip(old); return; }
            g.drawString(wrapped, r.x + 14, yy);
            yy += Math.max(12, fm.getHeight());
        }
        g.setClip(old);
```

```java
    ArrayList<String> contextInputPromptLines(PanelMode mode) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (mode == null) return lines;
        switch (mode) {
            case LOOK:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.EXAMINE, "examine selected tile", selectedLookNpc() != null || baseObjectAt(lookX, lookY) != null || world != null && world.inBounds(lookX, lookY), "select a visible tile first"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.INTERACT, "open interaction at selected tile", world != null && world.inBounds(lookX, lookY), "no selected tile"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "close look", true, ""));
                break;
            case INTERACT:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, "commit selected interaction", world != null && world.inBounds(lookX, lookY) && Math.abs(lookX - playerX) <= 1 && Math.abs(lookY - playerY) <= 1, "move adjacent first"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.PLAN_MOVE, "approach selected target", selectedInteractionApproachTile() != null, "already adjacent or no reachable approach tile"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "back out", true, ""));
                break;
            case INVENTORY:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, "use or equip selected carried item", selectedInventoryItemName() != null, "no carried item selected"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.INTERACT, "take, drop, or context item action", selectedInventoryItemName() != null, "no carried item selected"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "close inventory", true, ""));
                break;
            case BUILD:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, "confirm selected build placement", buildPlacementActive && pendingBuildRecipe != null, "choose a build and valid tile first"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.BUILD, baseClaimed ? "open construction and base tools" : "claim a room or open build tools", true, ""));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "cancel placement or close build", true, ""));
                break;
            case WORKBENCH:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, "run selected workbench action", selectedWorkerMachine() != null || hasBaseObject('w'), "build or select a machine first"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.INVENTORY, "check inputs and outputs", true, ""));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "close workbench", true, ""));
                break;
            case BASES:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, "use highlighted base action", baseClaimed, "claim a room first"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.BUILD, "return to construction tools", true, ""));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "close base management", true, ""));
                break;
            case TRADE:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CONFIRM, activeTrader != null ? "buy selected offer" : "choose conversation option", activeTrader != null && selectedTradeOffer() != null || activeConversationNpc != null, "no active trader or speaker"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.INVENTORY, "change selected sell item", true, ""));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "leave trade or conversation", true, ""));
                break;
            case MAP:
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.MOVE_LEFT, "pan or change map focus", world != null, "no map loaded"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.ZOOM_IN, "zoom map/world view where supported", worldZoomControlActive(), "zoom unavailable here"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.CANCEL, "close map", true, ""));
                break;

                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.LOOK, "inspect visible source", world != null, "no world loaded"));
                lines.add(contextPromptLine(InputAction.PLAN_MOVE, "plan around hazards or darkness", world != null, "no world loaded"));
```

```java
    void drawPanel(Graphics2D g) {
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.LOOK) {
            drawGame(g);
            drawLookDetailPanel(g);
            return;
        }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT) {
            drawGame(g);
            drawCombatTargetDetailPanel(g);
            return;
        }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.INTERACT) {
            drawGame(g);
            drawInteractDetailPanel(g);
            return;
        }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.SCAVENGE) {
            drawGame(g);
            drawScavengeTargetPanel(g);
            return;
        }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH) {
            drawGame(g);
            drawBuildDetailPanel(g);
            return;
        }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.CHARACTER) { drawModalScrim(g); drawCharacterDossierPanel(g); return; }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.FACTIONS) { drawModalScrim(g); drawFactionRelationsPanel(g); return; }

        if (panelMode == PanelMode.NEWS) { drawModalScrim(g); drawNewsArchivePanel(g); return; }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.SAVELOAD) { drawModalScrim(g); drawSaveLoadPanel(g); return; }
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.INFOPEDIA) { drawModalScrim(g); drawInfopediaPanel(g); return; }
        Rectangle modal = uiLayout().modal;
        g.setColor(new Color(6,7,7,246)); g.fillRect(modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, modal.x, modal.y, modal.width, modal.height, "inner");

        g.setFont(uiFont); g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        List<String> lines = panelLines();

    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:5813-5850

SHA256: a6c8bcef32f9264ed2e1174bcc79ab9400491e4d00b7bc03bac82d2679b1b0bd

```java
    void drawInventoryIconGrid(Graphics2D g, LinkedHashMap<String,Integer> stacks, int selectedIndex, int x, int y, int w, int h, String context) {
        Shape old = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(x, y, Math.max(1, w), Math.max(1, h));
        g.setColor(new Color(4,5,5,210));
        g.fillRoundRect(x, y, w, h, 8, 8);
        if (stacks == null || stacks.isEmpty()) {
            g.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Math.max(8f, smallFont.getSize2D()-2f)));
            g.setColor(new Color(128,112,80));
            drawUiTextLine(g, context.equals("target") ? "No visible floor/container stack." : "No carried item stacks.", x+8, y+22);
            g.setClip(old);
            return;
        }
        int cell = Math.max(34, Math.min(48, Math.max(1, w) / Math.max(3, Math.min(5, stacks.size()))));
        int gap = 6;
        int cols = Math.max(1, Math.max(1, (w + gap) / (cell + gap)));
        int i = 0;
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : stacks.entrySet()) {
            int cx = x + (i % cols) * (cell + gap);
            int cy = y + (i / cols) * (cell + gap);
            if (cy + cell > y + h) break;
            boolean sel = (i == selectedIndex);
            g.setColor(sel ? new Color(98,76,34,235) : new Color(12,14,13,235));
            g.fillRoundRect(cx, cy, cell, cell, 8, 8);
            g.setColor(sel ? optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT) : new Color(104,90,58));
            g.drawRoundRect(cx, cy, cell, cell, 8, 8);
            drawMiniStackIcon(g, e.getKey(), cx+4, cy+4, cell-8);
            int count = e.getValue() == null ? 1 : e.getValue();
            if (count > 1) {
                g.setFont(new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(8, Math.min(11, cell/4))));
                g.setColor(new Color(0,0,0,190));
                g.fillRoundRect(cx+2, cy+2, Math.min(cell-4, 20), 13, 5, 5);
                g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT));
                drawUiTextLine(g, "x" + count, cx+4, cy+12);
            }
            i++;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
    }
```

Name: handleInventoryStackPanelClick

```java
    boolean handleInventoryStackPanelClick(int mx, int my) {
        if (screen != Screen.PANEL || panelMode != PanelMode.INVENTORY) return false;
        int W=getWidth(), H=getHeight();
        int x=Math.max(36, W/2 - Math.min(880, W-72)/2);
        int y=Math.max(68, H/2 - Math.min(440, H-110)/2);
        int w=Math.min(880, W - x*2);
        int h=Math.min(440, H - y - 54);
        int gap=Math.max(12, scaled(12));
        int top=y+128;
        int bottomBoxH=Math.max(78, Math.min(108, h/4));
        int colH=Math.max(110, h - (top-y) - bottomBoxH - 26);
        int actionW=Math.max(150, Math.min(210, w/4));
        int invW=Math.max(180, (w - 52 - actionW - gap*2)/2);
        int targetW=Math.max(180, w - 52 - actionW - gap*2 - invW);
        int invX=x+24;
        int targetX=invX+invW+gap;
        LinkedHashMap<String,Integer> invStacks=displayedInventoryStacks();
        LinkedHashMap<String,Integer> targetStacks=currentTargetInventoryStacks();
        int hit = inventoryGridIndexAt(invStacks, invX+12, top+48, invW-24, colH-60, mx, my);
        if (hit >= 0) {
            selectedInventoryIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(hit, Math.max(0, invStacks.size()-1)));
            inventoryTargetColumnActive = false;
            inventoryItemDescriptionScroll = 0;
            logEvent("Inventory selection: highlighted carried stack " + selectedInventoryStackName() + ".");
            repaint();
            return true;
        }
        hit = inventoryGridIndexAt(targetStacks, targetX+12, top+48, targetW-24, colH-60, mx, my);
        if (hit >= 0) {
            selectedTargetInventoryIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(hit, Math.max(0, targetStacks.size()-1)));
            inventoryTargetColumnActive = true;
            inventoryItemDescriptionScroll = 0;
            logEvent("Inventory target: highlighted floor/container stack " + selectedTargetInventoryName() + ".");
            repaint();
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
```

```java
    void drawContractObjectiveMarker(Graphics2D g, int zx, int zy, int layerIndex, int px, int py, int cell) {
        ArrayList<FactionContract> matches = new ArrayList<>();
        for (FactionContract c : activeVisibleContracts()) {
            ContractZoneTarget target = contractZoneTarget(c);
            if (target != null && contractTargetOnCurrentMapLayer(target) && target.zoneX == zx && target.zoneY == zy) matches.add(c);
        }
        if (matches.isEmpty()) return;
        int pulse = (int)((System.currentTimeMillis() / 240L) % 4L);
        Graphics2D gg = (Graphics2D) g.create();
        gg.setStroke(new BasicStroke(2.0f + pulse));
        gg.setColor(new Color(255, 225, 95, 210));
        gg.drawRoundRect(px + 6 + pulse, py + 6 + pulse, Math.max(8, cell - 12 - pulse * 2), Math.max(8, cell - 12 - pulse * 2), 10, 10);
        gg.setFont(smallFont.deriveFont(Font.BOLD, Math.max(9f, smallFont.getSize2D() - 2f)));
        gg.setColor(new Color(20, 14, 4, 225));
        gg.fillRoundRect(px + 8, py + 8, Math.min(cell - 16, 94), 22, 8, 8);
        gg.setColor(new Color(255, 235, 120));
        gg.drawString(matches.size() == 1 ? "OBJECTIVE" : matches.size() + " OBJECTIVES", px + 14, py + 24);
        gg.dispose();
    }
```

```java
    void drawScrollableWrappedLines(Graphics2D g, java.util.List<String> lines, int x, int y, int w, int h, int scroll, String tag){
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        FontMetrics fm=g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH=Math.max(18,fm.getHeight()+3);
        java.util.List<String> flat=TextLayoutAuthority.wrapAllPixels(g, g.getFont(), lines, Math.max(12, w - 4));
        int visible=Math.max(1,h/lineH); int maxScroll=Math.max(0,flat.size()-visible); scroll=Math.max(0,Math.min(scroll,maxScroll));
        applyScrollValue(tag, scroll, false);
        Shape old=g.getClip(); g.setClip(x-4,y-4,w+8,h+8);
        int yy=y+lineH;
        for(int i=scroll;i<Math.min(flat.size(),scroll+visible);i++){
            String line=flat.get(i); g.setColor(line.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("invalid")||line.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("warning")?new Color(245,120,90):optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            g.drawString(line,x,yy); yy+=lineH;
        }
        g.setClip(old);
        int sbX=x+w+10, sbY=y, sbW=14, sbH=h;
        g.setColor(new Color(20,18,14,235)); g.fillRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        g.setColor(new Color(108,92,58)); g.drawRect(sbX,sbY,sbW,sbH);
        int th=maxScroll<=0?h:Math.max(28,h*visible/Math.max(visible,flat.size())); int ty=maxScroll<=0?y:y+(h-th)*scroll/maxScroll;
        g.setColor(tag.equals(activeScrollTag)?optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_HIGHLIGHT):new Color(220,190,105)); g.fillRect(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3));
        scrollRegions.add(new ScrollRegion(tag, new Rectangle(sbX, sbY, sbW, sbH), new Rectangle(sbX+2,ty+2,sbW-3,Math.max(6,th-3)), maxScroll, visible, scroll));
    }
```

```java
    String currentScrollableTag(){
        if(screen==Screen.CHARACTER) return jobDossierTab==0?"job-dossier":"job-list";
        if(screen==Screen.PANEL){
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.INVENTORY) return activeScrollTag != null && activeScrollTag.equals("inventory-info") ? "inventory-info" : "inventory";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.LOOK) return "look-stack";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.CHARACTER) return "character";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.FACTIONS) return "factions";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.BASES) return "bases";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.NEWS) return "infopedia-detail";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.MAP && mapTab==1) return "map-info";
            if(panelMode==PanelMode.INFOPEDIA) return activeScrollTag!=null && activeScrollTag.equals("infopedia-detail") ? "infopedia-detail" : "infopedia-list";
        }
        return "";
    }
```

```java
    ScrollRegion findScrollRegion(int mx,int my){
        for(int i=scrollRegions.size()-1;i>=0;i--){ ScrollRegion r=scrollRegions.get(i); if(r.track.contains(mx,my) || r.thumb.contains(mx,my)) return r; }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:28-36
Kind: method
Name: handleScrollbarClick
SHA256: 62b9871cc99c9c04117aea10cc139ebfd7a8e5fe3c69e09e9a9fa4abbcebf521

```java
    void handleScrollbarClick(int mx,int my){
        ScrollRegion r=findScrollRegion(mx,my);
        if(r==null) return;
        activeScrollTag=r.tag;
        if(r.maxScroll<=0){ applyScrollValue(r.tag,0,true); return; }
        if(r.thumb.contains(mx,my)){ scrollbarDragActive=true; scrollbarDragOffsetY=my-r.thumb.y; return; }
        int dir = my < r.thumb.y ? -1 : 1;
        applyScrollValue(r.tag, r.value + dir * Math.max(1,r.visibleLines), true);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:37-45

Name: handleScrollbarDrag
SHA256: 8ad5d94f81d14d6122ddcdf8d74cbd56f5d0617a2d612b426fb278c6dc521e60

```java
    void handleScrollbarDrag(int mx,int my){
        if(!scrollbarDragActive || activeScrollTag==null || activeScrollTag.isEmpty()) return;
        ScrollRegion target=null; for(ScrollRegion r:scrollRegions) if(r.tag.equals(activeScrollTag)){ target=r; break; }
        if(target==null || target.maxScroll<=0) return;
        int usable=Math.max(1,target.track.height-target.thumb.height);
        int rel=Math.max(0, Math.min(usable, my - scrollbarDragOffsetY - target.track.y));
        int value=(int)Math.round((rel/(double)usable)*target.maxScroll);
        applyScrollValue(target.tag, value, true); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void drawBuildDetailPanel(Graphics2D g) {
        UiLayout L = uiLayout();
        int x = Math.max(18, L.map.x);
        int w = Math.max(360, Math.min(L.map.width, L.command.x - x - 18));
        int h = panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH ? Math.max(190, Math.min(230, getHeight() / 3)) : Math.max(210, Math.min(250, getHeight() / 3));
        int y = Math.max(10, Math.min(18, L.map.y - h - 6));
        if (y < 10) y = 10;
        updatePendingBuildSummary();

        g.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, x, y, w, h, "inner");

        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(new Color(185, 225, 150));
        drawUiTextLine(g, panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH ? "SCRAP WORKBENCH / WORK MENU" : "BASE CONSTRUCTION", x + 14, y + 27);

            }

        lines.add("Cursor is room-bound. Select a construction from the right-side build menu, move with WASD/arrows, then press E to confirm.");
        lines.add("Pending: " + pendingBuildSummary);
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD) lines.addAll(constructionMenuGuidanceLines(pendingBuildRecipe));
        if (pendingBuildRecipe != null) lines.add(ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.semanticSummaryForName(pendingBuildRecipe.name));
        lines.add("Requirements use Mechanics + Intellect. Build time uses Strength + Agility. Failure risk is reduced by Intellect + Faith.");
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD) {
            lines.add(ConstructionValidationInspectionAuthority.compactLine(this));
        } else {
            FactionRecipeVariant v = selectedGeneratedProductionJob();
            lines.add(v == null ? "No controlled generated job selected." : ("Generated job: " + v.outputName + " | filters " + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.categoryFilterName(generatedJobCategoryFilterIndex) + "/" + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.readinessFilterName(generatedJobReadinessFilterIndex) + " | " + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.shortStatus(this, selectedWorkerMachine(), v)));
            lines.add(MachineOperationStatusBridge.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(StaffingLaborBridgeAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsReservationForecastAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsDeliveryIntentAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsStorageCandidateAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsSourceReservationAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsRouteIntentAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsRouteReadinessPreviewAuthority.compactSummary(this));
            lines.add(LogisticsManualHaulContractAuthority.compactSummary(this));
        }
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawClippedWrappedLines(g, lines, x + 14, y + 44, w - 28, h - 54, smallFont, false);
    }
```
