```java
    void drawInteractDetailPanel(Graphics2D g) {
        UiLayout L = uiLayout();
        int x = Math.max(18, L.map.x);
        int y = 12;
        int w = Math.max(360, L.command.x - x - 18);
        int h = Math.max(132, Math.min(168, L.map.y - 18));
        int tx = lookX, ty = lookY;
        BaseObject obj = baseObjectAt(tx, ty);
        char ch = (world != null && tx >= 0 && ty >= 0 && tx < world.w && ty < world.h) ? world.tiles[tx][ty] : ' ';
        updatePendingInteractionSummary();
        g.setColor(new Color(8, 8, 10, 238));
        g.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, x, y, w, h, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "interact-detail", x, y, w, h);
        g.setFont(uiFont);
        g.setColor(new Color(140, 230, 180));
        drawUiTextLine(g, "MECHANDRITE / INTERACT", x + 14, y + 28);
        String target = (obj != null ? obj.name + ": " + obj.description : describeTile(ch));
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add("Selected target | Adjacent use required | " + target);
        String summary = hoveredButtonDescription();
        if (summary == null || summary.isEmpty()) summary = pendingInteractionSummary;
        lines.add("Preflight: " + pendingInteractionSummary);
        if (!summary.equals(pendingInteractionSummary)) lines.add("Context: " + summary);
        lines.add("Move cursor: WASD/Arrows | Confirm: far-right command button/Enter | Leave: ESC");
        g.setFont(smallFont);
        g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
        drawClippedWrappedLines(g, lines, x + 14, y + 46, w - 28, h - 58, smallFont, false);
    }
```

```java
    String itemActionSummary(String item) {
        String low = item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (low.contains("coffee") || low.contains("stim") || low.contains("narcotic")) return "Wakefulness drug: reduces sleep need but adds cumulative endurance strain. Drop is always available.";
        if (low.contains("ration") || low.contains("food")) return "Can be consumed to restore food. Drop is always available.";
        if (low.contains("water") || low.contains("canteen")) return "Can be consumed to restore water. Drop is always available.";
        if (looksWearable(item)) return "Equip/disguise item: USE changes worn identity and defense, returning the previous outfit to inventory. Drop is available.";
        if (low.contains("scrap") || low.contains("detritus") || low.contains("machine") || low.contains("supplies")) return "Workbench/build material. USE converts carried construction supplies into internal supplies where applicable; workbench actions consume the rest.";
        if (low.contains("field dressing") || low.contains("injector") || low.contains("medicae")) return "Medical utility: USE reduces wounds/fatigue if available.";
        if (low.contains("data spike") || low.contains("keycard") || low.contains("lockpick") || low.contains("hacking tools") || low.contains("tool")) return "Tool item: automatically applies to doors, vaults, vending, and context checks while carried.";
        if (low.contains("leader journal")) return "Stolen intelligence: INN buys faction leader journals for major bounties; USE reviews the sell note.";
        if (low.contains("newspaper") || low.contains("paper mush")) return "News item: USE reads the INN issue or discovers that damp paper has won.";
        if (low.contains("radio") || low.contains("pict-screen") || low.contains("pict screen") || low.contains("television")) return "Broadcast receiver: USE monitors current INN radio/pict bulletins without needing a vending machine.";
        if (PortableLightProfile.isLightItem(item)) return "Portable light: USE activates/carries/wears it, DROP leaves an active light on the floor, THROW LIGHT tosses it ahead. Radius and burn time depend on the item.";
        if (low.contains("used food tin") || low.contains("ration wrapper")) return "Common arcology trash. Reserved recycling hooks may recover scrap or contamination value.";
        if (low.contains("map") || low.contains("survey")) return "Navigation utility: USE studies it and reduces local risk pressure.";
        return "No direct use action wired yet. Drop is available.";
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:750-788
Kind: method
Name: useUtilityInventoryItem
SHA256: 98db6643ef20d14bd67a3a88f7afd6a9481ae8091e4b115f1db3880ed7ee9245

```java
    void useUtilityInventoryItem(String item) {
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) { logEvent("Cannot use " + item + ": no carried copy found."); return; }
        String low = item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        int oldWounds=wounds, oldFatigue=fatigue, oldSuspicion=suspicion, oldHeat=gangHeat;
        if (isMedicalUseItem(low)) {
            removeInventoryAtWithTrace(idx);
            applyMedicalItemEffect(item, low, oldWounds, oldFatigue);
        } else if (low.contains("leader journal")) {
            logEvent("STOLEN JOURNAL: " + item + ". INN bounty estimate " + InnBountyApi.journalBounty(item, null) + " Concord Script. Sell at an INN bureau or newspaper dispenser contact point.");
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("sealed bank lockbox") || low.contains("stock certificate") || low.contains("house gold")) {
            logEvent("BANK HEIST LOOT: " + item + " is valuable, incriminating, and best sold through a trader, faction contact, or noble heist quest profile. Merely staring at it does not launder it.");
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("newspaper") || low.contains("paper mush")) {
            readInventoryNewspaper(item);
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("radio") || low.contains("pict-screen") || low.contains("pict screen") || low.contains("television")) {
            listenToPortableBroadcastReceiver(item);
            return;
        } else if (PortableLightProfile.isLightItem(item)) {
            usePortableLightItem(item);
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("data spike") || low.contains("keycard") || low.contains("lockpick") || low.contains("hacking tools") || low.contains("tool roll") || low.contains("tool bundle")) {
            logEvent(item + " is now active as a carried tool. Door, vault, vending, and interaction checks automatically read it from inventory; it is not consumed by manual USE.");
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("trade chit") || low.contains("concord script")) {
            logEvent(item + " is currency. Use TRADE/VEND/SERVICE menus to spend it; direct USE would merely annoy the coin.");
            return;
        } else if (low.contains("map") || low.contains("survey")) {
            removeInventoryAtWithTrace(idx); suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - 1); gangHeat = Math.max(0, gangHeat - 1);
            logEvent("Studied " + item + ". Suspicion " + oldSuspicion + "->" + suspicion + ", gang heat " + oldHeat + "->" + gangHeat + ". The route ledger grows less stupid.");
        } else {
            logEvent("No direct use action wired for " + item + ". Try DROP, WORKBENCH, TRADE, or context interaction.");
            return;
        }
        DebugLog.audit("INVENTORY_USE_UTILITY", "item=" + item + " wounds=" + oldWounds + "->" + wounds + " fatigue=" + oldFatigue + "->" + fatigue + " suspicion=" + oldSuspicion + "->" + suspicion + " heat=" + oldHeat + "->" + gangHeat + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("uses a utility item"); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    List<String> panelLines() {

                break;
            case INTERACT:

                break;
            case SCAVENGE:
                lines.add("Targeted scavenging submenu. Current target: " + selectedScavengeTarget);

                for (int ii=inventoryScroll; ii<Math.min(stackLines.size(), inventoryScroll+visibleInv); ii++) lines.add(stackLines.get(ii));
                if (stackLines.size() > inventoryScroll + visibleInv) lines.add("  ... more item stacks below ...");
                lines.add("Base storage items: " + baseStorage.size() + " stack(s pending storage grouping)");

                lines.add("Targeting feedback reports range, fire mode, hit %, obstruction/cover penalty, intervening entities, doors/features, and shield mitigation estimates.");

                    lines.add("Trader also buys the carried item currently selected in INVENTORY.");
                } else if (activeConversationNpc != null) {
                    lines.add("Conversation: " + activeConversationNpc.name + " — " + activeConversationNpc.role + " — " + activeConversationNpc.faction.label);
                    lines.add("Standing: " + conversationStandingLine(activeConversationNpc));
                    lines.add("Speaker read: " + conversationSpeakerReadLine(activeConversationNpc));
                    lines.add("Current topic: " + conversationBranch);
                    lines.addAll(conversationChoiceGuidanceLines(activeConversationNpc));
                    lines.add("Contracts: " + contractBoardLine(activeConversationNpc.faction));
                    for (FactionContract c : factionContracts) if (!c.completed && c.faction == activeConversationNpc.faction) lines.add("  " + c.longLine());
                    lines.add("Every choice is recorded in the in-game event log.");
                } else {
                    lines.add("No active trader or conversation. Depot fallback functions remain available if invoked from old content.");
                }
                lines.add("Last trade: " + lastTradeReport);
                lines.add("All buy, sell, rumor, and haggle choices are recorded in the in-game event log.");
                break;
            case MAP:
                if (mapTab == 0) {
                    lines.add("DIEGETIC SECTOR MAP — SLICE " + MapLayerSurfaceAuthority.label(mapLayerView));
                    lines.add("World intent: 3x3 sectors, each with 3x3 zones per floor, 10 floors, and sewer B-layers.");
                    lines.add("Current sector: " + (atlas == null ? "unknown" : atlas.sectorX + "," + atlas.sectorY) + " of 3x3. Current zone: " + (world == null ? "unknown" : world.zoneCoordText()) + ". Current layer: " + (world == null ? "unknown" : world.layerText()) + ".");
                    lines.add("Use LAYER -/+ buttons or mouse wheel to scroll through floor/sewer slices.");
                    if (world != null) lines.addAll(world.diegeticMapLines(mapLayerView));
                } else {
                    lines.add("ROOM TYPE / SCAVENGE INTEL");
                    lines.add("Room descriptors are separated from the map so the map remains readable.");
                    if (world != null) lines.addAll(visibleRoomIntelLines());
                }
                break;
            case LOG:
                lines.add("Recent event log:");
                lines.addAll(eventLog);
                break;
            case SAVELOAD:
                lines.add("LOAD / SAVE PERSISTENCE");
                lines.add("Manual saves: 4 slots. Autosaves: 5-column surface; first two are currently hourly and zone-transition autosaves.");
                lines.add("Autosave cadence: every in-game hour (" + AUTOSAVE_INTERVAL_TURNS + " turns) and on completed zone transitions; death screen intentionally does not overwrite autosaves.");
                lines.add("Run state: seed=" + seed + " turn=" + turn + " time=" + timeText() + " player=" + playerX + "," + playerY + " score=" + PlayerDefeatAndScoreAuthority.score(this));
                lines.add("World location: " + worldLocationSummary());
                lines.add("Character: " + (active == null ? "no active run" : active.name + " / " + active.job));
                lines.add("Base: " + (baseClaimed ? baseX + "," + baseY + " room=" + claimedRoomId : "none"));
                lines.add("Run counters: kills=" + runKills + " crafted=" + runCrafted + " talked=" + runNpcTalkedTo + " unconscious=" + runUnconsciousEvents + " knowledge=" + unlockedKnowledges.size() + " zones=" + visitedZoneInstances.size());
                lines.add("");
                lines.add("MANUAL SAVE SLOTS");
                for (int i=1;i<=SAVE_SLOT_COUNT;i++) lines.add("  " + saveSlotSummary(i));
                lines.add("");
                lines.add("AUTOSAVE SLOTS");
                lines.add("  AUTO 1: " + saveSlotSummary(AUTOSAVE_HOURLY_SLOT));
                lines.add("  AUTO 2: " + saveSlotSummary(AUTOSAVE_ZONE_SLOT));
                lines.add("  AUTO 3: empty");
                lines.add("  AUTO 4: empty");
                lines.add("  AUTO 5: empty");
                lines.add("");
                lines.add("Inventory=" + inventory.size() + " Storage=" + baseStorage.size() + " BaseObjects=" + baseObjects.size() + " NPCs=" + (world==null?0:world.npcs.size()) + " MapObjects=" + (world==null?0:world.mapObjects.size()));
                lines.add("Tracked: player, atlas coordinates, visited zone records, faction standings, hostility timers, item-instance containers, base objects, current-zone NPCs, shops, persistent stock, machine locks, production queues, and survival/defeat counters.");
                break;
            case INFOPEDIA:
                lines.add("Infopedia is rendered by the dedicated tabbed logic Engine panel.");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("No panel selected.");
        }
        return lines;
    }
```

```java
    void applyOptions() {
        double f = DisplayDensityAuthority.clampScale(options.fontScale / 100.0f);
        DisplayDensityAuthority.applyGlobalSwingTextScale(options);
        titleFont = new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(20, (int)Math.round(36*f)));
        uiFont = new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(10, (int)Math.round(16*f)));
        smallFont = new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(8, (int)Math.round(12*f)));
        asciiFont = new Font("Monospaced", Font.BOLD, Math.max(8, (int)Math.round(13*f)));
        renderScaling.applyOptions(options);
        if (timer != null) timer.setDelay(options.targetTimerDelayMs());
        frameLimiter.configure(options);
        DebugLog.audit("DISPLAY_DENSITY", DisplayDensityAuthority.auditSummary(options));
        DebugLog.audit("DISPLAY_RESOLUTION", DisplayResolutionAuthority.auditSummary(options));
        DebugLog.audit("OPTIONS", "Applied options fontScale=" + options.fontScale + " uiScale=" + options.uiScale + " sfx=" + options.sfxVolume + " music=" + options.musicVolume + " conversation=" + options.conversationVolume + " windowMode=" + options.windowMode + " resolution=" + options.resolutionLabel() + " downscale=" + options.downscaleLabel() + " targetFps=" + options.targetFpsLabel() + " frameLimited=" + options.frameLimitLabel() + " renderQuality=" + options.renderQualityLabel() + " reducedMotion=" + options.reducedMotion + " artQuality=" + options.artQualityLabel() + " generatedPayload=" + options.generatedAssetPayloadRootShortLabel() + " mapTileSize=" + options.mapTileSizeLabel() + " worldZoom=" + options.worldZoomLabel());
    }
```

```java
    void changeWorldZoom(int delta, String source) {
        int before = options.worldZoomIndex;
        options.worldZoomIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(GameOptions.WORLD_ZOOM_LABELS.length - 1, options.worldZoomIndex + delta));
        if (options.worldZoomIndex != before) {
            options.save();
            sounds.play("tab", options);
            logEvent("Viewport zoom " + options.worldZoomLabel() + " via " + source + ".");
            DebugLog.audit("VIEWPORT_ZOOM", "source=" + source + " index=" + options.worldZoomIndex + " label=" + options.worldZoomLabel() + " mode=" + screen + "/" + panelMode + " state=" + stateSummary());
        } else {
            logEvent("Viewport zoom already at " + options.worldZoomLabel() + ".");
        }
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void drawGraphicsDropdownPopupFrame(Graphics2D g) {
```

Source: gamepanel-shard8.txt:750-767
Kind: method
Name: drawClippedWrappedLines
SHA256: dfa558f8063b0336cff1cf514f668e383bf29ab0160d010e32631ab6e689bdb7

```java
    void drawClippedWrappedLines(Graphics2D g, java.util.List<String> lines, int x, int y, int w, int h, Font font, boolean centered) {
        if (lines == null || w <= 4 || h <= 4) return;
        Font oldFont = g.getFont();
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setFont(font == null ? smallFont : font);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        int lineH = Math.max(12, fm.getHeight() + 1);
        g.setClip(x, y, Math.max(1, w), Math.max(1, h));
        int yy = y + fm.getAscent();
        for (String line : TextLayoutAuthority.wrapAllPixels(g, g.getFont(), lines, Math.max(8, w - 4))) {
            if (yy > y + h) { g.setClip(oldClip); g.setFont(oldFont); return; }
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            if (centered) g.drawString(line, x + (w - fm.stringWidth(line)) / 2, yy); else g.drawString(line, x, yy);
            yy += lineH;
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
        g.setFont(oldFont);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard8.txt:769-785

Name: drawFrameWrappedCenteredText
SHA256: ec4f4ae17bb6f07422d97a2fa526c4b72041981403b32ac66e42ba1bc539322c

```java
    void drawFrameWrappedCenteredText(Graphics2D g, String text, int x, int y, int w, int h, Font font) {
        if (text == null) text = "";
        Font oldFont = g.getFont();
        g.setFont(font == null ? uiFont : font);
        FontMetrics fm = g.getFontMetrics();
        java.util.List<String> lines = TextLayoutAuthority.wrapPixels(g, g.getFont(), text, Math.max(8, w - 8));
        int lineH = Math.max(fm.getHeight() + 6, 22);
        int totalH = lines.size() * lineH;
        int yy = y + Math.max(fm.getAscent(), (h - totalH) / 2 + fm.getAscent());
        for (String line : lines) {
            if (yy > y + h) break;
            g.setColor(optionColor(GameOptions.TEXT_MAIN));
            center(g, line, x + w / 2, yy);
            yy += lineH;
        }
        g.setFont(oldFont);
    }
```

```java
    boolean buttonIsModalInteractive(ButtonBox b) {
        if (b == null) return false;
        if (screen == Screen.OPTIONS && graphicsDropdown >= 0) return isGraphicsDropdownButton(b);
        if (screen == Screen.SECTOR_AUDIT && auditZoneDropdownOpen) return isZoneAuditDropdownButton(b) || (b.label != null && b.label.startsWith("ZONE:"));
        return true;
    }
```

```java
    void activateSelectedButton() {
        if (!buttons.isEmpty() && selectedButton >=0 && selectedButton < buttons.size()) {
            ButtonBox b = buttons.get(selectedButton);
            if (!buttonIsModalInteractive(b)) { sounds.play("panelClose", options); return; }
            sounds.play("button", options);
            runGuarded("BUTTON", "activate selected button " + b.label, b.action);
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard8.txt:891-910
Kind: method
Name: targetPanelCursorFromMouse
SHA256: 1bcb0b2d0c5ec8dc157ef85101d16c3a7d889e8dc2e673f279cdb1dad2d20210

```java
    void targetPanelCursorFromMouse(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null || !world.inBounds(tx, ty)) return;
        if (panelMode == PanelMode.LOOK) {
            lookCursorActive = true;
            lookX = tx; lookY = ty;
            lookStackIndex = 0; lookStackScroll = 0;
            activeScrollTag = "look-stack";
        } else if (panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT) {
            combatCursorActive = true;
            combatX = tx; combatY = ty;
            lastTargetingReport = targetingSolutionAt(tx, ty).summary;
        } else if (panelMode == PanelMode.INTERACT) {
            interactCursorActive = true;
            lookX = tx; lookY = ty;
            clampInteractCursorToAdjacent();
            lookStackIndex = 0;
            updatePendingInteractionSummary();
        }
        DebugLog.audit("MOUSE_TARGETING", "panel=" + panelMode + " tile=" + tx + "," + ty + " source=virtual-map");
    }
```

```java
    @Override public void mouseClicked(MouseEvent e) {

            // any button underneath them can receive it. This prevents selecting a
            // dropdown value while also triggering an obscured option button.
            for (int i=buttons.size()-1;i>=0;i--) {

                    sounds.play("button", options);
                    runGuarded("MOUSE", "click dropdown " + b.label, b.action);
                    repaint();
                    return;

            repaint();
            requestFocusInWindow();
            return;

                requestFocusInWindow();
                repaint();
                return;

        requestFocusInWindow();
    }
```

```java
    void handleKeyPressed(KeyEvent e) {
        lastInputMillis=System.currentTimeMillis();
        int code=e.getKeyCode();
        if (eulaGateActive) {
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_ENTER || code == KeyEvent.VK_A) { acceptEulaGate(); repaint(); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_ESCAPE || code == KeyEvent.VK_Q || code == KeyEvent.VK_X) { requestApplicationExit("EULA declined by key"); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_PAGE_DOWN) { scrollEulaGate(1, true); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_PAGE_UP) { scrollEulaGate(-1, true); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_DOWN || code == KeyEvent.VK_S) { scrollEulaGate(1, false); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_UP || code == KeyEvent.VK_W) { scrollEulaGate(-1, false); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_HOME) { eulaScroll = 0; repaint(); return; }
            if (code == KeyEvent.VK_END) { eulaScroll = Math.max(0, eulaMaxScroll); repaint(); return; }
            return;

        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_F1 && (screen == Screen.GAME || screen == Screen.PANEL)) { toggleTacticalSlate(); return; }
        if (code == KeyEvent.VK_Y && screen != Screen.EDITOR) { openChatWindow(); return; }
        if (screen == Screen.GAME && firstPersonRenderViewport.handleKeyPressed(this, code)) { repaint(); return; }
        if (worldZoomControlActive() && (code == KeyEvent.VK_HOME || code == KeyEvent.VK_END)) {
            changeWorldZoom(code == KeyEvent.VK_HOME ? 1 : -1, code == KeyEvent.VK_HOME ? "HOME" : "END");
            return;
        }
        if (screen==Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) {

            return;
        }
        if (screen==Screen.CAPTURE) {

            return;

                characterNameEditActive = false;
                repaint();
                return;

                if (c != null && c.name != null && !c.name.isEmpty()) { c.name = c.name.substring(0, c.name.length()-1); refreshNameLockedCandidateState(c); }
                repaint();
                return;
            }

                if (c != null) { c.name = ""; refreshNameLockedCandidateState(c); }
                repaint();
                return;
            }
            return;

        if (code==KeyEvent.VK_ESCAPE) {

            else if (screen==Screen.PANEL) closePanel();

            beginInteractMode(); repaint(); return;

        if (code==KeyEvent.VK_F) { beginCombatTargeting(); repaint(); return; }
        if (code==KeyEvent.VK_G) { beginExplosiveTargeting(); repaint(); return; }

            case KeyEvent.VK_LEFT: case KeyEvent.VK_A: dx=-1; break;
            case KeyEvent.VK_RIGHT: case KeyEvent.VK_D: dx=1; break;
            case KeyEvent.VK_W: dy=-1; break;
            case KeyEvent.VK_S: dy=1; break;
        }
        if (dx!=0 || dy!=0) {
            queueOrExecuteMovementInput(dx, dy);
        }
        repaint();
        sanityCheck("KEY_END");
    }
```

```java
    void processUnifiedInputRegistry(long now) {
        // Keyboard retains the existing direct KeyEvent path. This timer consumer only
        // translates GAMEPAD source states so a controller release cannot erase a held key.
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.PAUSE, InputSource.GAMEPAD) || inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.CANCEL, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) {
            if (screen==Screen.GAME && manualMovementPlanActive) cancelManualMovementPlan("gamepad cancel");
            else if (screen==Screen.GAME) setScreen(Screen.PAUSE);
            else if (screen==Screen.PANEL) closePanel();
            else if (screen==Screen.PAUSE) setScreen(Screen.GAME);
            else setScreen(Screen.MENU);
            repaint();
            return;
        }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.CONFIRM, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) {
            if (screen == Screen.GAME && manualMovementPlanActive) confirmManualMovementPlan();
            else if (screen == Screen.INTRO_CRAWL) continueFromIntroCrawl();
            else if (screen == Screen.ZONE_SPLASH) continueFromZoneSplash();
            else activateSelectedButtonUniversal();
            repaint();
        }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.INVENTORY, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && screen == Screen.GAME) { openPanel(PanelMode.INVENTORY); return; }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.CHARACTER, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && screen == Screen.GAME) { openPanel(PanelMode.CHARACTER); return; }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.LOOK, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && screen == Screen.GAME) { interactCursorActive=false; lookX=playerX; lookY=playerY; lookCursorActive=true; openPanel(PanelMode.LOOK); return; }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.PLAN_MOVE, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && screen == Screen.GAME) { beginManualMovementPlan(); return; }
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.ZOOM_IN, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && worldZoomControlActive()) changeWorldZoom(1, "gamepad bumper");
        if (inputRegistry.consumePressed(InputAction.ZOOM_OUT, InputSource.GAMEPAD) && worldZoomControlActive()) changeWorldZoom(-1, "gamepad bumper");
        if (now < nextUnifiedInputRepeatMillis) return;
        int dx = 0, dy = 0;
        if (inputRegistry.isActiveFromSource(InputAction.MOVE_LEFT, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) dx--;
        if (inputRegistry.isActiveFromSource(InputAction.MOVE_RIGHT, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) dx++;
        if (inputRegistry.isActiveFromSource(InputAction.MOVE_UP, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) dy--;
        if (inputRegistry.isActiveFromSource(InputAction.MOVE_DOWN, InputSource.GAMEPAD)) dy++;
        if (dx == 0 && dy == 0) return;
        nextUnifiedInputRepeatMillis = now + 125L;
        if (screen == Screen.GAME && world != null && manualMovementPlanActive) {
            nudgeManualMovementPlan(Integer.compare(dx, 0), Integer.compare(dy, 0));
        } else if (screen == Screen.GAME && world != null) {
            queueOrExecuteMovementInput(Integer.compare(dx, 0), Integer.compare(dy, 0));
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.LOOK && world != null) {
            lookCursorActive = true;
            lookX = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.w-1, lookX+Integer.compare(dx, 0)));
            lookY = Math.max(0, Math.min(world.h-1, lookY+Integer.compare(dy, 0)));
            lookStackIndex = 0;
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.INTERACT && world != null) {
            moveInteractCursor(Integer.compare(dx, 0), Integer.compare(dy, 0));
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && panelMode == PanelMode.COMBAT && world != null) {
            moveCombatCursor(Integer.compare(dx, 0), Integer.compare(dy, 0));
        } else if (screen == Screen.PANEL && (panelMode == PanelMode.BUILD || panelMode == PanelMode.WORKBENCH) && buildPlacementActive && world != null) {
            moveBuildCursor(Integer.compare(dx, 0), Integer.compare(dy, 0));
        } else if (!buttons.isEmpty()) {
            moveSelectedButton(dy < 0 || dx < 0 ? -1 : 1);
        }
        repaint();
    }
```
